[\[2a.1\]]rnams dang /_nam mkha' lding rnams dang /_klu rnams dang /_gnod sbyin rnams dang /_mi 'am ci rnams dang /_srin po rnams dang /_dri za rnams dang /_rig sngags 'chang grub pa rnams dang /_'byung po rnams dang /_log 'dren rnams dang /_

[\[2b.1\]]ba/_bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gi dbang du bgyis te/_gnod pa dang drang bas bkug cing drangs te tho btsams na/_bcom ldan 'das bskyab tu gsol/_de skad ces gsol ba dang /_bcom ldan 'das kyis thams cad kyi steng gi dkyil 'khor yangs pa ston pa'i mchog gi blo gros 
[\[2b.2\]]dang /_blo dang /_las dang /_las kyi mtha' dang ldan pa/_sa chen po las sa gzhan thob pa rgyal tshab tu nye ste/_chos kyi rgyal srid la dbang bskur ba'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rjes su dgongs par mdzad pa tsam gyis 'ongs te/_rdo rje'i zo ma ltar dpung mgo yangs pa/_rdo 
[\[2b.3\]]rje ltar mkhregs pa'i cod pan 'od zer 'tsher ba can/_rdo rje'i dpung rgyan dang ldan pa/_lus mkhregs shing sra ba dang /_lag na rdo rje dang /_zhags pa dang /_lag na brtan po 'bar ba thogs pa/_rdo rje phur bu sra bas rab tu 'joms par byed pa/_mthu chen po g.yog bzhi 'bum lnga khri

[\[5a.1\]]gzungs sngags rnams rab tu brjod du gsol/_lag na rdo rjes smras pa/_bram ze'i khye'u rab tu nyon la yid la zung shig dang /_nga yis bde gshegs khro bo thams cad kyis rtag tu brjod pa'i yang snying 'di rab tu smras so/_/na mo ra t+na tra yA ya/_na ma sh+ca N+Ta badzra pA 
[\[5a.2\]]Na ye/_ma hA yak+Sha se nA ba ta ye/_ta d+ya thA/_oM ha ra ha ra badzra/_ma tha ma tha badzra/_d+hu na d+hu na badzra/_da ha da ha badzra/_ba tsa ba tsa badzra/_d+ha ra d+ha ra badzra/_dA ra ya dA ra ya badzra/_dA ru Na dA ru Na badzra/_ts+tshin+da ts+tshan+da badzra/_b+hin+da b+hi n+da badzra/_hU~M phaT thA/_na ma sh+tsa N+Da badzra kro d+hA ya/_hu lu hu 
[\[5a.3\]]lu/_tiSh+Tha tiSh+Tha/_ban+d+ha ban+d+ha/_ha na ha na/_a mr-i te hU~M phaT thA/_bram ze'i khye'u gang la la zhig gis bde gshegs bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i cha bzung ste/_khro bo thams cad kyi rdo rje'i tshig 'di rab tu smra zhing /_ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas rdo rje phra mo grangs med pa sprul te phyogs bcur 
[\[5a.4\]]spros na/_sems can thams cad kyi bag chags ngan pa byang /_tshe dang bsod nams rab tu rgyas te/_dgra dang /_dug dang /_dus ma yin par 'chi ba las rnam par thar nas/_gang zhig gis dmigs pa'i rgol ba ngan pa la rtsi ma gi ta sprin gyis bshig pa'am/_skyu ru ra rlon 
[\[5a.5\]]pa gser gyis gzhibs pa bzhin du dmigs te/_rdo rje'i tshig 'di smra zhing /_rdo rje phra mo spros pas de dag gi phung po lnga dbang po lnga myur du brlag par 'gyur ro/_/lhas smras na lha'i zla ba gcig gam/_lo ldan lha ma yin mgo 'gas par 'gyur ro/_/dge slong gis smras

[\[5b.2\]]bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa//_kun dga' bo rigs kyi bu'am/_rigs kyi bu mo gang la la zhig gis gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje bcu'i ming shes sam/_rus shes sam/_gsang sngags shes pa de la byad kyis mi tshugs so/_/
[\[5b.3\]]gnod sbyin dag rnam par 'tshe bar mi 'gyur ro/_/srin po rnams dang /_lhag ma za ba rnams dang /_bdug pa za ba rnams 'tshe bar mi 'gyur ro/_/phyis 'jog pa rnams kyang gnod par mi 'gyur ro/_/ta d+ya thA/_u ki ri ma ki ri/_mi rI tsa pA sha pa ri/_u li me/_mi li me/_i 
[\[5b.4\]]li me/_mi li me/_i li me/_mi li me/_i li ma li me/_hik+ke/_d+hik+ke/_huk+ke/_d+hu d+hu re/_pra d+ha re/_a laM pha le/_phA laM pha le/_khu khu me ti ku me tu me/_khi ri khi ri/_sA d+ha sA d+ha/_sarba bak+k+wa le/_ban d+ha ma bak+k+wa le/_kun dga' bo gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po 
[\[5b.5\]]lag na rdo rje bcu po 'di dag la rtag tu bdag gi phyi bzhin du 'brang bar gyur nas bdag gnyid log pa dang /_myos pa dang /_rab tu myos pa yang bsrung ba dang /_yongs su bskyab pa dang /_yongs su gzung ba dang /_yongs su bskyang ba dang /_zhi ba dang /_bde legs su 'gyur bar byed par

[\[6a\]]
[\[6a.1\]]yongs su bskyang ba dang /_zhi ba dang /_bde legs su 'gyur bar byed par bcom ldan 'das kyis bkas gsol ba thob shig_/gsang sngags kyi gzhi 'di rnams grub par gyur cig swA hA/_tad+ya thA/_sa ra sa ra Ne swA hA/_de la lag na rdo rje bcu bo de dag

[\[14b.1\]]'di dus gsum du 'chang ngam/_klog gam/_yid la byed dam/_rjes su dran par byed na dbul ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad las thar bar 'gyur ro/_/lo nyes pa byung ba'i tshe/_stobs po che lan bdun bklags na/_sprin chen po las char 'bab bo/_/gal te char mi 'bab 
[\[14b.2\]]na sprin gyi lha rnams kyi srog skam par 'gyur ro/_/klu'i rgyal po nag po dang /_klu'i rgyal po 'khor lo dang /_klu'i rgyal po mtha' yas la sogs pa klu'i rgyal po rnams kyis sprin chen po las char 'bebs so/_/gal te char mi 'bebs na srog skam par 'gyur ro/_/gong du 
[\[14b.3\]]smos pa'i cho ga bzhin du phyogs kyi cha'am/_klung gi ngogs sam/_rgya mtsho'i 'gram mam/_mtsho'i 'gram mam/_mchod rten gyi gnas su byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rje la mchod pa chen po byas te/_tsan+dan dmar po dang /_ka ra bI ra'i 
[\[14b.4\]]me tog dang /_pad+ma dmar po dang /_a ti muk+ta ka'i me tog dang /_tsam pa ka'i me tog dang /_rgyal mtshan dang /_ba dan dmar po la sogs pa dang /_bum pa spos chus bkang ba la sogs pas mchod pa chen po byas te/_gang mdo sde 'di 'chang 
[\[14b.5\]]ba dang /_klog pa de g.yul ngo thams cad du zhugs kyang pha rol gyis mi tshugs par 'gyur ro/_/sems can thams cad dga' bar 'gyur ro/_/bkra mi shis pa thams cad las rnam par grol bar 'gyur ro/_/stobs po che rgyal mtshan gyi rtse mo la btags te g.yul 
[\[14b.6\]]ngor song na pha rol gyis mi tshugs par 'gyur ro/_/gsang sngags gro ga la bris te spyi bor btags nas g.yul ngor mtshon cha rnams me tog bzhin du ltung bar 'gyur ro/_/de nas bdud des bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas te phyogs gcig tu 
[\[14b.7\]]'dug nas stobs po che zhes bgyi ba ci lags zhes gsol pa dang /_bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/_stobs po che zhes bya ba ni de bzhin gshegs pa'o/_/stobs po che zhes bya ba ni chos so/_/stobs po che zhes bya ba ni chos kyi phung po'o/_/stobs po che 
[\[15a\]]
[\[15a.1\]]zhes bya ba ni chos kyi tshul lo/_/stobs po che zhes bya ba ni theg pa chen po'o/_/stobs po che zhes bya ba ni lag na rdo rje'o/_/de nas bdud sdig can gyis smras pa/_gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje legs so legs so/_/skyabs su mchi'o/_/sangs 
[\[15a.2\]]rgyas dang /_chos dang /_dge 'dun la skyabs su mchi'o/_/bcom ldan 'das legs so legs so/_/dge bsnyen gyi yan lag gzung bar bgyi'o/_/bde dang thar dang mtho ris dang /_/mkhas pa dag dang sems can ni/_/dam pa kun la phan pa'i phyir/_/stobs po 
[\[15a.3\]]che ni gzung bar bgyi/_/de nas bdud sdig can chos la dga' zhing yid bde ba dang rangs par gzigs nas/_bcom ldan 'das kyis 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/_/rig sngags kyi rgyal po stobs po che'i mdo sde 'di ni sems can dmyal ba dang /_dud 'gro 
[\[15a.4\]]dang /[ {]yi dgas [,]yi dwags [}]dang /_gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sdug bsngal las thar bar byed pa'o/_/de bskal pa stong phrag nyi shur lha'i rgyal po byed par 'gyur ro/_/bskal pa mtha' yas par gling bzhi la dbang ba'i 'khor los sgyur bar 'gyur ro/_/bla na med pa yang dag 
[\[15a.5\]]par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la 'jog par byed do/_/rig sngags kyi rgyal po stobs po che'i snying po 'di ni gtsang sbra can nam/_gtsang sbra med pa'am/_smyung bar byas pa'am/_smyung bar ma byas pa'am/_'khrig pa'i chos la sten pa la'ang 'grub par byed do/_/de la 
[\[15a.6\]]bar chad du mi 'gyur ro/_/de nas rab 'byor 'khor de nyid na 'dug par gyur pas bcom ldan 'das rig sngags kyi rgyal po stobs po che ji ltar gzung bar bgyi/_dam pa ni ci zhig stsol ces gsol ba dang /_bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/_lag na rdo rje la dri ba dris 
[\[15a.7\]]shig_/rab 'byor gyis smras pa/_lag na rdo rje rig sngags kyi rgyal po stobs po che ji ltar gzung bar bgyi/_dam pa ni ci zhig sbyin par byed/_lag na rdo rjes smras pa/_'bru sbyin par byed do/_/gos sbyin par byed do/_/dngul sbyin par byed do/_/gser sbyin par 
[\[15b\]]
[\[15b.1\]]byed do/_/ba lang sbyin par byed do/_/dam pa gang 'dod pa'i dam pa de sbyin par byed do/_/rab 'byor gyis smras pa/_spyi'i 'bras bu zhes bya ba'am/_lag na rdo rjes smras pa/_rab 'byor de de bzhin te/_sems can nyon mongs pas bsgribs pa rnams la ni 'bras bu'i 
[\[15b.2\]]dus su gnas so/_/'bras bu'i dus kyi yon tan gyi don du gnas so/_/yon tan gyi don gyis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi lam la 'jog par byed do/_/rab 'byor gyis smras pa/_lag na rdo rje legs so legs/_/gsang ba'i mtshan nyid ldan pa 
[\[15b.3\]]ste/_/stobs po che ni shes rab ldan/_/gsang ba'i mtshan nyid phun sum tshogs/_/spyi nas dbang bskur yid kyang gzhungs/_/mtshan dang yang dag ldan pa ste/_/sbyin dang tshul khrims shes rab che/_/rdzu 'phrul che zhing stobs kyang che/_/dbang cher grags shing bsod 
[\[15b.4\]]nams che/_/yon tan rtse mo stobs po che/_/mdo sde 'di la dbang bskur phyir/_/sangs rgyas brgyad stong der gshegs so/_/byang chub sems dpa' lag na rdo rjes mdo sde 'di nyid kyis mi 'jigs pa'i lag pa spyi bor bzhag ste/_dge ba byed par 'gyur ro/_/gang gis 
[\[15b.5\]]gzungs sngags 'di sa'am/_ri'am/_klung gi ngogs sam/_rgya mtsho'i 'gram du bcangs na 'jigs pa thams cad kyis 'jigs pa med par 'gyur ro/_/de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' lag na rdo rjes 'di skad ces gsol to/_/su mdo sde 
[\[15b.6\]]'di 'chang ba dang /_klog pa dang /_gzhan dag la yang rgya cher yang dag par rab tu ston pa de bro nad ma mchis par lo brgya 'tsho bar 'gyur ro/_/lag na rdo rjes yang gsol pa/_chos kyi rnam grangs 'di'i ming ci lags/_'di ji ltar gzung bar bgyi/_/bcom 
[\[15b.7\]]ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/_mdo sde 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa zhes bya bar zung shig_/chos kyi nyi ma zhes bya bar yang zung shig_/don thams cad grub pa zhes bya bar yang zung shig_/de bzhin 
[\[16a\]]
[\[16a.1\]]gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi sprin ces bya bar yang zung shig_/sdig pa thams cad byang bar byed pa'i gzungs sngags zhes bya bar yang zung shig_/rig sngags 'chang thams cad grub pa'i rgyal po zhes bya bar yang zung shig_/shes rab kyi pha rol tu 
[\[16a.2\]]phyin pa zhes bya bar yang zung shig_/chos kyi dbyings de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngon du 'gro ba zhes bya bar yang zung shig_/rig sngags kyi rgyal po stobs po che zhes bya bar yang zung shig_/gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje su mdo sde 'di 'dzin pa dang /_'chang 
[\[16a.3\]]ba dang /_klog pa dang /_yi ger 'drir 'jug pa dang /_bsti stang du byed pa dang /_bla mar byed pa dang /_ri mor byed pa dang /_mchod par byed pa de/_'das pa dang /_ma 'ongs pa dang /_da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas dang /_byang chub sems dpa' rnams la mchod pa 
[\[16a.4\]]byas par 'gyur ro/_/'das pa dang /_ma 'ongs pa dang /_da ltar byung ba rnams kyi mchod rten sku gdung dang bcas pa la mchod pa byas par 'gyur ro/_/lag na rdo rjes gsol pa/_bcom ldan 'das legs so legs so/_/shin tu zab pa'i chos bstan pa dang /_cho 
[\[16a.5\]]'phrul gyi yon tan gyi rgyan gyi chos bstan pa gzung bar bgyi'o/_/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/_lag na rdo rje rigs kyi bu'am rigs kyi bu mo gang mdo sde 'di 'chang ba de la sdang ba'i sems can rnams chu 'gram gyi shing ltar ma rungs par 'gyur ro/_/spos 
[\[16a.6\]]dang /_me tog dang /_bdug pa dang /_rgyal mtshan dang /_ba dan sna tshogs la sogs pas mchod pa byas na bsod nams kyi phung po dpag tu med pa dang ldan par 'gyur ro/_/de la bar chad mi 'byung bar 'gyur ro/_/mdo sde 'di gnas gang yang rung ba na 'chang na lha 
[\[16a.7\]]dang mir bcas pas mchod pa byed par 'gyur ro/_/rig sngags kyi rgyal po stobs po che/_bgegs dang /_rnam par log 'dren thams cad 'ching ba yid la byed na sangs rgyas brgyad stong dang /_byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams dang /_drang srong chen 
[\[16b\]]
[\[16b.1\]]po rnams dang /_lha dang /_klu dang /_dri zar bcas pa rnams dgyes dga'o/_/stobs po che'i gzungs sngags 'di la dgyes pa'i dus kyi tshe/_de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/_/gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje su mdo sde 'di la gus 
[\[16b.2\]]par mi byed pa de dag sems can dmyal ba chen po brgyad po dag tu skye bar 'gyur ro/_/gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje su mdo sde 'di la gus par byed pa dang /_rim gro byed pa dang /_mchod pa byed pa de bsod nams kyi phung po dpag tu med pa dang ldan par 'gyur ro/_/yi 
[\[16b.3\]]ge 'dri 'am/_chig mnyan na phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur ro/_/lag na rdo rjes gsol pa/_thub pa'i chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa/_shin tu phra ba/_shin tu zab pa/_bsam gyis mi khyab pa la sems can rnams kyi nang nas gang log par 
[\[16b.4\]]sems pa de myos par 'gyur ro/_/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/_gsang ba pa'i bdag po lag na rdo rje sems can rnams kyi don gyi phyir mdo sde 'di bshad par bya'o/_/sems can thams cad kyi sgrib pa bsal ba dang /_zhi bar bya ba dang /_rgyas par bya ba dang /_
[\[16b.5\]]dbang bskur ba dang /_bkra mi shis pa thams cad las thar bar bya ba dang /_dpal gyis byin gyis brlab par bya ba dang /_sdig pa thams cad byang bar bya ba dang /_sems can thams cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob par bya ba'i phyir bshad 
[\[16b.6\]]par bya'o/_/de'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa brgyad stong dang bar mdzad nas/_de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa la lan gsum bskor ba mdzad de/_thal mo sbyar nas legs par rab tu bshad pa legs so zhes mngon par dgyes par mdzad do/_/de nas de bzhin gshegs

[\[17a.1\]]rjes sdang ba bgegs dang /_rnam par log 'dren thams cad kyi snying 'dar zhing 'gul bar mthong ngo /_/dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/_/gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje drag po la phyag 'tshal lo/_/ta d+ya thA/_oM ha na ha na badzra/_

[\[17a.5\]]su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to/_/bcom ldan 'das 'du byed thams cad kyi mi rtag pa'i mtshan nyid ji lta bu lags/_bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/_byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa nyon

[\[18a.1\]]pa'i sprul pa zhes bya'o/_/mdo sde 'di 'tsho zhing sdod na de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa yang 'tsho zhing sdod de/_mtshan nyid des na de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa zhes bya'o/_/de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyang mdo sde 'di nyid la phyag 'tshal te/_

[\[18a.5\]]byed pa'o/_/de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rjes 'di skad ces gsol to/_/bcom ldan 'das mtshan nyid gang gis na mdo sde 'di chos kyi dbyings sngon du 'gro ba zhes bgyi/_bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/_
[\[18a.6\]]rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad byung nas zhag sum cu rtsa gnyis lon pa'i nyin mo ri btang bzung chen por mdo sde 'di nyid kyi chos bstan te/_mtshan nyid des na chos kyi dbyings sngon du 'gro ba zhes bya'o/_/mdo sde 'di nyid kyi mthus sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems

[\[19a.1\]]mtshungs par stobs kyi pha rol gnon par 'gyur ro/_/stobs po che pha rol gnon pa'i khro bo 'di'i mthus bdag dang sems can thams cad/_swa sti swa sti/_sid d+hi sid d+hi swA hA/_bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang /_'phags pa

[\[23b.2\]]bya mtshan nyid rnam shes dang /_/ye shes nyid ni mngon sum du/_/skye ba nyid la the tsom med/_/de nas rgya chen sbyor ba'i gtso/_/'khor lo'i cho ga bshad par bya/_/gro ga ras sam shing shun la/_/gur gum gi wa tsan+dan bcas/_/pu ka ser pos 'khor lo ni/_/
[\[23b.3\]]rtsibs bcu pad+ma'i steng du bri/_/mtha' nas me yi phreng bas bskor/_/pad+ma'i 'dab ma bcu la ni/_/phyogs bcu kun du bcing ba yi/_/rdo rje la sogs bcu po bri/_/de yi rgyab tu phyogs bcu rnams/_/bcing ba'i sngags ni rim bzhin bri/_/'khor lo'i rtsibs rnams bcu po la/_/
[\[23b.4\]]hU~M gnyis bar du bsgrub bya'i ming /_/bsrung ba dang bcas bri bar bya/_/phyogs bzhir sngags dang phyag rgya dang /_/'khrul 'khor gcod dang 'ching ba dang /_/'gugs pa'i sngags su bcas pa bri/_/gzhan yang mtshams rnams drug por ni/_/lha dang klu dang lha min gyi/_/gnod 
[\[23b.5\]]sbyin grul bum la sogs pa/_/bcing ba drug po bri bar bya/_/lte bar bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan ni/_/skyil krung thugs kar thal mo sbyar/_/mdzes pa'i gos ldan bri bar bya/_/de rjes gsang sngags phreng ba nyid/_/stong phrag gcig tu brjod byas nas/_/de rjes bstod 
[\[23b.6\]]pas bstod byas te/_/gser sogs dril nas lus sam mgul/_/gang bde'i gnas su gdags par bya/_/des ni rnal 'byor bsrung don du/_/ji ltar bsam pa kun 'grub ste/_/'jigs pa brgyad po med par byed/_/de nas gzhan yang rgyal po'i ras/_/gser 
[\[23b.7\]]la tsan+dan ga bur dang /_/dri zhim rnams kyis byas nas ni/_/rgyu skar rgyal gyi nyi ma la/_/gur gum gyis ni 'khor lo bri/_/dbus su pad+ma 'dab brgyad pa'i/_/phyi rol mu khyud gsum ldan pa'i/_/pad+ma'i lte bar bsgrub bya'i gzugs/_/yan lag rdo rjes mtshan pa bri/_/de la 
[\[24a\]]
[\[24a.1\]]snying po'i sngags kyis bskor/_/de rjes lte ba'i mu khyud la/_/steng 'og bcing ba'i sngags kyis bri/_/phyogs mtshams sngags rnams 'dab ma la'o/_/phyi rol mu khyud dang por ni/_/rtsa ba'i sngags ring dgod par bya/_/gnyis par 'od kyi ra ba bri/_/dri zhim 
[\[24a.2\]]dkyil 'khor steng bzhag ste/_/rang nyid lha yi sbyor rdzogs bya/_/thugs ka'i sa bon 'od kyis ni/_/nam mkhar 'khor lo sbyangs byas te/_/yi ge hU~M gi rnam par bsam/_/de yongs gyur las sku tshogs sgom/_/de dbus shes rab rnam par bsam/_/zla dbus steng du hu~M las 
[\[24a.3\]]ni/_/'khor lo rtsibs ldan bsgom par bya/_/der ni yi ge'i rnam pa ni/_/mar me lta bu gsal dmigs la/_/mkha' 'gro ma dang dbyer med bya/_/rang snying sa bon las byung ba'i/_/gsang sngags stong phrag bzlas byas nas/_/gser sogs dril nas lus sam mgul/_/
[\[24a.4\]]btags na 'jigs pa brgyad las skyob/_/thams cad du ni bsrung bar nges/_/yungs kar ba yi rnam lnga dang /_/dUr ba'i snye mar bcas pa la/_/gsang sngags stong phrag bzlas nas ni/_/rgan mo ming med sbyor ba yis/_/gnas gsum thig le byas bsrung na/_/tshe ni stong phrag 
[\[24a.5\]]du mar 'phel/_/ku sha ba mar yungs kar til/_/gsang sngags stong phrag bzlas byas te/_/shis par gyur pa'i nyi ma la/_/mchod rten spyi bor gdags byas na/_/'go ba'i nad rnams 'chad par 'gyur/_/khrag dang khro chur bcas pa la/_/gsang sngags stong phrag 
[\[24a.6\]]gsum bzlas te/_/zla ba gzas gzung dus su ni/_/nye bsnyen rdzogs par byas nas ni/_/rdzas ni shin tu spa byas te/_/lha tshogs gnod pa gang dmigs pa'i/_/snying gar sngags ni bsnun byas na/_/gang dmigs bgegs ni rnam par 'jig_/ras bal gsar 
[\[24a.7\]]par gyur pa la/_/shes rab mtshan ldan khrus byas te/_/shis pa'i nyi ma la bkal nas/_/bcings pa'i grangs kyis mdud byas te/_/stong phrag gcig gi sngags bzlas nas/_/lus sam mgul lam spyi bor gdags/_/des ni tshe lo stong phrag thub/_/
[\[24b\]]
[\[24b.1\]]yang na rang lus rnams bsgrims nas/_/chu yi tshogs kyis dag byas te/_/nyi shu rtsa gcig grangs ldan par/_/gzungs kyi phreng ba brjod byas na/_/gsar phyag lag tu ma blangs shing /_/bden bral phyi rol ma song bar/_/gzhan gyi 'jigs pa ma bsal zhing /_/
[\[24b.2\]]tshe lo brgya ni rtsa brgyad par/_/rims nad tsam yang mi gnod do/_/gos dang zas dang snod spyad dang /_/sman la sogs pa'i rdzas rnams ni/_/mi 'khrugs rgyal po'i phyag rgya yis/_/bsrungs na cis kyang mi shod de/_/seng chen rngam pa'i stabs kyis ni/_/'ug pa'i sgra 
[\[24b.3\]]gsum brjod byas na/_/phyi rol rig sngags stong phrag ni/_/du mas cis kyang mi tshugs so/_/klu yi dbang po gnas lugs kyis/_/rtse gcig rdo rje'i phyag rgya bcas/_/de nas gsang sngags gsum brjod na/_/nad dang gdon la sogs pa sel/_/ri bong nu ma'i 
[\[24b.4\]]mtshams byas nas/_/hU~M gis mnan pa'i sngags kyis ni/_/dmigs med ting 'dzin yid brtan zhing /_/'dis kyang gnod pa las bsrung 'gyur/_/phyi rol sogs pa kun spangs nas/_/snang ba yid kyis bslabs byas te/_/mi snang ba la mngon dmigs nas/_/bsrung ba 
[\[24b.5\]]rnams kyi dam pa bshad/_/de nas gzhan yang sbyor ba bshad/_/dur khrod la sogs 'jigs gnas sam/_/mtsho dang mtshe'u dang dgon gnas dang /_/gnas dang skyed mos tshal chen dang /_/me tog tshal lam yul 'khor ljongs/_/chu yi 'gram mam shing gcig 
[\[24b.6\]]gam/_/yang na rang gi khyim nyid du/_/maN+Dal legs par byugs pa la/_/brten nas lha yi sbyor ba sgrub/_/ras ris la sogs mdun byas te/_/bde ba'i stan la skyil krung gis/_/bsdad nas mnyam gzhag brtsam par bya/_/tha mal sbyangs pa'i lus kyis ni/_/thar 
[\[24b.7\]]pa chen po thob 'gyur te/_/gzhan du de ltar ma yin no/_/sa gzhi shin tu nyams dga' zhing /_/legs par bkod pa'i ri bo la/_/nags tshal shin tu sdug pa la/_/bsil ba'i chu rgyun 'babs pa'i phyogs/_/rnam bkod me tog tshal gseb tu/_/shar du sgo bstan 
[\[25a\]]
[\[25a.1\]]khang pa la/_/sngags bzhis mtshams bcings cho ga yis/_/gsal khung dang bcas brtsigs pa'i phyogs/_/snyan pa'i bya yis sgra sgrogs shing /_/dri zhim spos ngad ldan pa la/_/dril bu sil sil sgra snyan sgrogs/_/lda ldi gos kyi phreng bas dkris/_/lhag 
[\[25a.2\]]pa'i 'du 'dzi rnam spangs nas/_/spyod pa mthun pa'i grogs dang ni/_/bde bar byang chub bsgrub par bya/_/'on kyang gnas dang grogs la sogs/_/rnal 'byor yid 'jug phyir brtsam ste/_/mtha' dag spangs pa'i pha rol na/_/lhag pa'i byang chub ma mchis so/_/bde dang sdug bsngal 
[\[25a.3\]]sna tshogs rnams/_/rang ga sems las 'byung mod kyi/_/sems rtog ma lus spang ba las/_/ngas ni chos gzhan 'ga' ma bshad/_/de bas sems rtog sna tshogs rnams/_/spang bar bya phyir sna tshogs thabs/_/sngags dang phyag rgya ting 'dzin dang /_/sbyor ba rgya chen rnams 
[\[25a.4\]]bshad do/_/drag po sgrub pa'i thabs 'ga' ni/_/rig pa'i khro mos mnyan par gyis/_/sa gzhi bdud rtsi lnga yis byugs/_/me yi dkyil 'khor sa bon bcas/_/dur khrod pha gus bri bar bya/_/der ni pho mo thod pa la/_/phyi rol dmar nag tshon gyis byugs/_/nang du 
[\[25a.5\]]sna tshogs rdo rje ni/_/mu khyud gsum ldan bri bar bya/_/dbus su rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma'i/_/snying po sngags bcas bri bar bya/_/rdo rje rwa ni thams cad la/_/hU~M bri mu khyud gnyis phreng sngags/_/gsum par khro bo'i sngags bri'o/_/thod pa kha sbyor nang du ni/_/ske tshe yungs 
[\[25a.6\]]kar btsan dug dang /_/lan tshwa khrag dang sha chen dang /_/rkang rjes sa la sogs pa blugs/_/gcer bu rnal 'byor skra bshig nas/_/lha yi sbyor ldan lhor bltas nas/_/zhabs kyis thod pa'i 'khor lo ni/_/mnan te sngags phreng brjod par bya/_/khro bo chen po'i sbyor ba yi/_/
[\[25a.7\]]mnyam bzhag nas ni stong phrag tu/_/bzlas pa mtshan phyed par byas na/_/bsad pa nyid la the tshom med/_/dur khrod ras la 'khor lo ni/_/dbus su me yi dkyil 'khor can/_/rtsibs brgyad mu khyud gsum ldan pa/_/dbus su snying po sngags rnams la/_/hU~M 
[\[25b\]]
[\[25b.1\]]gnyis par du bsgrub bya'i ming /_/bsad pa nyid dang ldan par bya/_/mu khyud gnyis pa phreng sngags kyang /_/ming dang bsad par ldan pa'o/_/gsum pa khro bo'i sngags bris te/_/'khor lo mchod cing byin brlabs nas/_/dgra gzugs sor brgyad snying gar gzhug_/

[\[25b.3\]]byang chub yan lag las/_/dur khrod khrag gis 'khor lo bri/_/gu gsum brtsegs pa'i gzugs bris te/_/dbus su dgra ming gsang sngags bcas/_/rtsibs la bcu gnyis bar du ni/_/ming dang bsad pa bcas pa bri/_/mu khyud dang po'i sngags phreng yang /_/rgyas 
[\[25b.4\]]ba'i yan lag ldan par bri/_/spra tshil gzugs brnyan sor brgyad pa'i/_/snying gar bcug nas skra yis dkri/_/rnal 'byor pa yi nyal ba'i zhabs/_/mgo bo lhor bstan gzhag par bya/_/chu shel ma mthong bar du ni/_/nyi shu rtsa gcig sngags brjod nas/_/mi yi rdo 
[\[25b.5\]]rje'i dar gyis brgyan/_/sdang byed sa steng 'dir mi gnas/_/klu yi gnas su grags pa'am/_/chu yi rdzing la sogs 'gram du/_/dkyil 'khor ba yi rnam lngas byugs/_/pad+ma dmar po'i ri mo la/_/lte ba rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma/_/gser gyi mdog can thal mo sbyar/_/
[\[25b.6\]]klu yi gdengs ka bdun ldan pa/_/zla ba'i dkyil 'khor steng gnas pa/_/shin tu bltas pas gnas par bya/_/dga' bo nyer dga' 'jog po dang /_/mtha' yas dung skyong rigs ldan gzugs/_/pad+ma pad chen rnams byas te/_/dkar dang ser dang ljang ba dang /_/

[\[26a\]]
[\[26a.1\]]snod du dgram par bya/_/gza' dang rgyu skar rnams dga' zhing /_/klu rnams bde ba'i sems thob shog_/lha rnams yid ni mnyam bzhag nas/_/snying rje'i blo chen skye bar shog_/lha klu gnod sbyin dri za sogs/_/byang chub sems chen dang ldan nas/_/

[\[26a.5\]]bcas pa yi/_/'khor lo thod pa'i gzugs bris la/_/pags pa gnyis kyis dkris byas pa/_/zla gam bye brag dkyil 'khor la/_/brten pas dbye ba'i sbyor ba rdzogs/_/mtshal dang tsan+dan ga bur bsres/_/zla gam dbyibs kyi dkyil 'khor la/_/snying po dbang 
[\[26a.6\]]gi sbyor bar bcas/_/nub tu bltas nas bsgrubs pa yi/_/lha yi dbang po dbang du 'gyur/_/rgyud kyi khyad par sbyor ba'o/_/dri yi rgyal po sna tshogs kyis/_/shing gi lo ma dkar po la/_/rdo rje rgya gram gnyis brtsegs kyi/_/phyogs kyi rwa rnams hU~M gis spras/_/

[\[26b\]]
[\[26b.1\]]dang 'brel ba spang /_/thal ba chu dang yungs kar la/_/sngags kyi phreng ba bzlas byas te/_/sprin la sogs pa 'khrugs pa'i tshe/_/gtor ba tsam gyis 'chad par 'gyur/_/'bru mar yungs kar ser po la/_/sngags nas lus la byugs tsam gyis/_/phran tshegs nad rnams

[\[26b.3\]]byos/_/ser sna spangs shing g.yo sgyu med/_/dul la dpa' brtul bzod pa che/_/mkhas shing rig pa brtson 'grus bzang /_/sngags la mkhas pas sbyin sreg brtsam/_/thab ni nyi shu sor tshad la/_/phyed brkos kha phyir rdo rje ni/_/rtse gsum dur khrod tshon gyis bri/_/
[\[26b.4\]]phyi rol phyag rgya rnam bkod nas/_/dri zhim me tog gcal du bkram/_/der ni mchod cing bsreg pa'i rdzas/_/tshogs nas rdzas rnams bsang gtor bya/_/bong bu rnga mo'i ril ma dang /_/gsal shing cher bcas shing la me/_/sa bon las skyes spar bar bya/_/der ni rdo rje 
[\[26b.5\]]lu gu rgyud/_/bskyed pa'i cho ga rdzogs byas nas/_/mchod cing bstod nas der rjes su/_/ske tshe yungs kar btsan dug dang /_/rus phye sha chen til nag po/_/dang bcas sbyin sreg stong phrag gcig_/phreng ba'i sngags kyis sbyor bar bya/_/thog ma tha mar mar chen

[\[26b.7\]]bcas/_/ser por byas la stong phrag ni/_/gcig gis 'phral du rengs par byed/_/sbrul rta ne'u le ma he'i sha/_/bya rog 'ug sha stong phrag gcig_/bsregs pas bsgrub bya 'byer bar nges/_/bra bo 'bras bu ra sha khrag_/stong phrag gcig gis lkugs par 'gyur/_/rnga

[\[27a.1\]]mo bya rog rgan po'i sha/_/sA lu dmar til dkar po dang /_/yungs kar ser po la sogs pa/_/stong du bsregs pas skrod par byed/_/'bru lnga smad 'tshong rang byung gis/_/nam phyed nub tu kha bltas byug_/me tog pad+ma dang bcas pa'i/_/kha dog dmar

[\[27b\]]
[\[27b.1\]]sngags gtsad par byed pa'i sngags so/_/rig pa'i rgyal po bla med ni/_/gsang chen 'di las 'byung bar 'gyur/_/gsang chen rgyud 'di ngo mtshar te/_/rmad byung bas ches rmad du byung /_/bstan pa'i snying po gsang chen 'di/_/gsungs pa'i de ma thag tu ni/_phyogs

[\[27b.4\]]chos kyi dbang phyug grags pas bsgyur ba'o//[ {D759}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_badzra tuN+Da nA ma nA ga sa ma ya/_bod skad du/_rdo rje mchu zhes bya ba klu'i dam tshig go/_/thams cad mkhyen pa la phyag 'tshal 
[\[27b.5\]]lo/_/de nas bcom ldan 'das grong khyer chen po g.yog 'dor na bzhugs te/_'khor 'dus pa chen po 'jog po la sogs pa klu'i 'khor dang /_lha dang mi'i tshogs kyi 'khor chen po la sems can rnams kyi don chen po'i phyir te/_bsam pa dang re ba thams cad 
[\[27b.6\]]yongs su skong ba bde bar byed pa'i chos ston to/_/de nas grong khyer de nas bram ze'i khye'u khyab ma spyan zhes bya ba phyug pa nor che ba/_longs spyod che ba/_rdzas dang yo byad mang po phun sum tshogs pa/_rig byed dang rig byed kyi yan lag gi pha rol tu phyin pa/_sngags

[\[28a\]]
[\[28a.1\]]rgyun dbab cing klu dgug par bya'o zhes smras te/_des me'i sbyin sreg bya bar bshams nas til dang /_'bras dang /_yungs kar rnams 'bru mar tsha ba dang bsres te sbyin sreg byed do/_/de nas klu mi srun pa zhig gi gzugs byas te/_des lcags 
[\[28a.2\]]kyi phur bu la bsngags nas klu'i spyi bor btab pa dang /_klu'i spyi bo gas nas sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba chen por gyur to/_/klu de yang cher 'khrugs te khros nas skad cig thang cig yud tsam de la klus khyab par byed pa'i shugs kyis cher gnod cing rdul 'byung ba'i 'od zer tsha ba rang

[\[83a\]]
[\[83a.1\]]chen po yang dag shes de nas lha ma yin gyi sa gnyis pa la gnas pa mgul phreng gis sgra gcan la smras pa/_sgra gcan khyod g.yul las brtan pa thob bam/_bde bar log gam zhes dris pa dang /_sgra gcan gyis smras pa/_kho bo'i ni ngal bso

[\[83b.1\]]dbang po'i grong khyer blta na sdug dbrog par bya'o/_/rgyal chen ris bzhi pa rnams 'bangs su bya'o zhes smras nas/_rang gi yul nas dpung gi tshogs chen po sgra gcan dang mgul phreng dang bcas pa snga ma bas brgya 'gyur gyis lhag pa ri rab kyi steng du phyin to/_/de'i tshe lha'i

[\[92a.1\]]grangs 'di rigs kyi bu khyed rnams nyon cig_/gnod sbyin chen po'i snying po 'di dkyil 'khor dang /_phyag rgya dang /_sngags dang gsang sngags chen po shin tu ngo mtshar ba dang /_shin tu rmad du gyur pa de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis gsungs pa/_

[\[101a\]]
[\[101a.1\]]ba'i sngags kyi rtog pa gsungs pa/_gang gis lo ma btsos pa za ba dang /_bsod snyoms kyis 'tsho zhing 'bum phrag gsum bzlas par bya'o/_/de nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i mdun du rgya che ba'i mchod pa byas nas stong phrag brgyad du bzlas pa byas na nor 
[\[101a.2\]]mang po rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/zla ba drug tu chu nang du chu'i sbyin sreg byas na stong phrag brgya rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin dkar gsum gyi gtor ma dang mchod pa phul la/_a shwat+tha'i yam shing zho dang mar dang sbrang rtsis sbags nas stong phrag brgyad du sbyin sreg byas na bar 
[\[101a.3\]]snang las sgra thos pa'am/_yid la 'dod pa'i rig pa 'dzin pa'i 'bras bu 'grub pa dang /_sems kyis byas pas tshogs par 'gyur ro/_/de bzhin du las tshogs gzhan yang 'grub ste/_ring bsrel dang bcas pa'i mchod rten la/_'bum phrag gcig bzlas nas/_dkar po 
[\[101a.4\]]dang nag po'i phyogs la bsod snyoms za zhing re mos kyis smyung bar gnas nas gtor ma dang mchod pa cho ga bzhin byin nas til nag mang po la zho dang mar dang sbrang rtsis sbags la stong phrag brgyad du sbyin sreg byas na grong gi mchog bcu gnyis rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/bag med pas 
[\[101a.5\]]las ma grub na stong phrag bcu'i nang nas grong gcig rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/chu bo'i 'gram du nor bu bzang po bzhag nas mar dang 'o thug za zhing mchod rten gdung dang ldan pa la 'bum phrag gcig bzlas nas/_gnam stong la mtshan mo smyung bar gnas pas/_dz+wa ti'i me tog 
[\[101a.6\]]la stong phrag brgyad du re re la mngon par bsngags nas mchod rten la phul na nang par phyugs stong phrag ster bar 'gyur ro/_/bsod snyoms za zhing rigs gtsang ma la dus gsum du khrus byed cing 'bum phrag gcig tu bzlas nas/_nag po'i phyogs kyi brgyad la mtshan 
[\[101a.7\]]mo smyung bar gnas la 'dzam bu'i yam shing la me sbar la/_nag pus pa zho dang mar dang sbrang rtsis sbags nas stong phrag brgyad du sbyin sreg byas pa dang /_mngar gsum gyi bshos gtsang ma dang gtor ma byin nas sbyin sreg yongs su rdzogs pa dang /_bram ze'i 
[\[101b\]]
[\[101b.1\]]gzugs kyis 'ongs nas nga yis ci byed ces smra bar byed do/_/de la smra ba dong tse lnga byin cig ces smras pa dang /_de ltar bya'o zhes zer nas mi snang bar gyur te nyin re bzhin du ster bar 'gyur ro/_/lhag ma med par zad par bya'o/_/pad+ma skyes pa mtsho'i 'gram du phyin te chu 
[\[101b.2\]]dang bcas pa'i phye za ba'am/_yang ci ltar rnyed pa'i zas za zhing nor bu bzang po kha phyir bstan par bzhag la gsol ba btab nas/_ji srid du stong phrag brgya rdzogs par pad+ma'i sbyin sreg byas na/_de'i rting la dpal mo 'ongs te 'ongs pa de la pad+ma nye bar phul nas dri dang bcas 
[\[101b.3\]]pa'i chu'i arga byin na/_des smras pa bu gcig ci bya zhes smras na/_sgrub pa pos smra bar bya ste/_gter mang po bdag la rab tu stsol cig_/de ltar bya'o zhes zer nas mi snang bar 'gyur ro/_/de nas gang du 'gro ba der khyer nas byin pa de zad pa med par 'gyur ro/_/nor bu bzang 
[\[101b.4\]]po'i mdun du zla ba phyed du bzlas nas ci srid zla ba nya'i nub mo smyung bar gnas pas/_sha med pa'i gtor ma byin nas/_de nas nor bu bzang po'i snying gar ming med bzhag nas ci srid du bzlas pa de srid du g.yo bar 'gyur ro/_/de nas nyin re bzhin du dong tse lnga lnga ster bar 'gyur 
[\[101b.5\]]ro/_/lhag med par zad par bya'o/_/dur khrod chen por phyin nas dur khrod kyi thal ba la mchod rten byas te/_bsod snyoms za zhing dus gsum du khrus byas nas 'bum phrag gsum du bzlas la/_/nag po'i phyogs kyi bcu bzhi la mtshan mo smyung bar gnas pas/_bcom 
[\[101b.6\]]ldan 'das la rgya che ba'i mchod pa byas nas lhag ma med par rab tu zad par bya'o/_/dur khrod chen por nor bu bzang po la sha ta puSh+pa phul la/_a ka ru dang du ru ska bsres pa'i bdug pa phul te/_gdong phyin ci log tu bzhag nas ci srid mtshan phyed pa de srid du bzlas so/_/
[\[101b.7\]]de nas sha za'i bdag po rang 'ongs pa dang sngar bzhag pa'i gtor ma phul la/_'khor rnams la chang yang dbul/_de nas sgrub pa pos gsol ba btab par bya'o/_/de nas de nga mgu'o zhes smra'o/_/sgrub pa pos smras pa/_nyi ma re re g.yog re re byin cig_/de ltar bya'o 
[\[102a\]]
[\[102a.1\]]zhes zer nas mi snang bar 'gyur ro/_/de nas mang ga gzhug pa la sogs pa rab tu sbyin to/_/gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pas las kyi tshogs bya ba gsungs pa/_ri'i rtse mor 'dzegs te khru gang tsam gyi nor bu bzang po bzhag nas 'o ma dang 'o thug za zhing 
[\[102a.2\]]dus gsum du khrus byed cing 'bum phrag gsum du bzlas nas/_de nas dkar po'i phyogs kyi nya la thug pa'i mtshan mo gsum du smyung bar gnas nas/_nor bu bzang po la rgya che ba'i mchod pa byas pa dang /_gtor ma'i cho ga rgya che ba byas nas ku sha'i chun po dag byed nas/_
[\[102a.3\]]ci srid sgra grag pa de srid du bzlas pa bya'o/_/de nas de ma thag tu gnod sbyin thams cad nye bar 'ongs nas/_de rnams la me tog dmar po dang /_dri dmar po dang /_arga sbyin par bya'o/_/du ru ska'i bdug pa yang bdug par bya'o/_/de nas gnod sbyin des legs so zhes 
[\[102a.4\]]bya ba byin nas smras pa/_ngas khyod la ci byed ces zer ba dang /_de nas de la smras pa dang /_nyin re bzhin mngag gzhug rab tu byin cig_/de ltar bya'o zhes zer nas mi snang bar 'gyur ro/_/de la sogs pa bsam gtan tsam gyis gnas pa la ma mthong bar 'khor gyis 
[\[102a.5\]]bskor nas gnas so/_/gang dang gang 'dod pa de dang der khang pa brtsegs pa dang /_lha'i bzhon pa sprul te stong phrag gcig dang bcas pa la rab tu 'dod pa la rab tu 'dod pa'i zas rnams ster bar 'gyur ro/_/nyin re bzhin du gnod sbyin mor sprul zhing 'ongs nas tho 
[\[102a.6\]]rangs kyi dus su 'gro bar 'gyur ro/_/de nyid kyi tshe lo stong du 'gyur ro/_/rgya mtsho'i 'gram du nor bu bzang po'i gzugs brnyan bzhag ste/_bsod snyoms za zhing 'bum phrag gsum bzlas nas dkar po phyogs kyi tshes lnga la thug par nub gsum du smyung bar 
[\[102a.7\]]gnas pas rgya mtsho chen po dang nye bar phyin nas/_ji srid rgya mtsho chen po rang 'ong ba de srid kyi bar du bzlas par bya'o/_/mdun du rgya mtsho chen po rang 'ongs pa de la dri dang me tog gi mchod pa phul la/_a ka ru'i bdug pas bdugs la/_kye rig pa 'dzin pa 
[\[102b\]]
[\[102b.1\]]mchog gang khyod la rab tu sbyin pa smra'o/_/des smras pa/_rgya mtsho chen po rung thogs pa med pa 'gro bar gyis/_de ltar bya zhes zer ba nas mi snang bar 'gyur ro/_/de nas rgya mtsho la zhugs nas/_rgya mtsho na yod pa'i nor bu rin po che blangs nas 'byung bar 'gyur ro/_/
[\[102b.2\]]rgya mtsho na yod pa'i klu rnams kyang dbang du 'gyur ro zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pas bka' stsal to/_/de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pas yang /_gnod sbyin gyi dbang po dbyangs snyan gyi sngags gsungs pa/_na mo rat+na tra yA ya/_
[\[102b.3\]]na mo ma Ni b+ha drA ya/_ma hA yak+Sha se na pa ta ye/_ma Ni ni swA hA/_rtsa ba'i dkar po'i phyogs kyi brgyad dam/_yang na dkar po'i bcu bzhi la nyin zhag gcig smyung bar gnas pas/_ro hi ta'i nya la ba'i lci ba dang /_mar gyis byugs nas stong phrag brgyad du sbyin 
[\[102b.4\]]sreg byas na dong tse brgya rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/gzhan yang nye bar mchod pa dang /_sngon du 'bum tsho gsum bzlas nas/_nya ma god pa la zho dang mar dang sbrang rtsis mngon par byugs nas stong phrag bcu sbyin sreg byas na dong tse stong phrag rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/ma grub na yang 
[\[102b.5\]]kA ra ShA pa Na stong phrag gcig rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/oM dzam b+ha ya dza len drA ya swA hA/_rtsa ba'i sngags so/_/de nas yang nor bu bzang po bsgrub par 'dod mchod sbyin gyi shing dkar po la nor bu bzang po'i gzugs brnyan byas la/_mchod pa chen po rab tu gnas pa byas nas/_
[\[102b.6\]]de'i mdun du yang a pa marga'i yam shing la mar dang sbrang rtsis byugs la 'bum phrag tu sbyin sreg byas na 'dod pa'i 'bras bu rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/be ta la'i me tog rnams kyis 'bum phrag tu sbyin sreg byas na/_gser srang stong rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/til dang 'bras thug 
[\[102b.7\]]po che'i sbyin sreg 'bum byas na gser srang stong rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/de ltar sha ta puSh+pa dang gu gul dang /_ku nad dang /_tsan+dan dkar po dang /_du ru ska la sogs pa de rnams re re 'bum du sbyin sreg byas na dong tse stong phrag rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/til dang 'bras kyi sbyin sreg 
[\[103a\]]
[\[103a.1\]]byas na rgyal po dbang du 'gyur ro/_/nye'u ci ltar 'tshong ba nyos la/_chu bo'i rgyun la lte ba nub tsam du chu'i nang du zhugs nas kha shar du bltas te sbyin sreg brgya byas na sum 'gyur gyi dong tse rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/ras bal gyi sa bon la mar dang sbrang rtsis 
[\[103a.2\]]byugs nas stong phrag gcig sbyin sreg byas na nyi ma bdun gyi bar la ras gcig rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/rtag tu bzlas na gos dang bza' ba rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/'bum du bzlas na dong tse lnga stong rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/'bum tsho gnyis bzlas na grong rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/'bum 
[\[103a.3\]]tsho gsum bzlas na longs spyod chen po rnyed par 'gyur zhing grong brgyad kyi bdag por 'gyur ro/_/be'u'i lci ba la sbyin sreg stong byas na ba lang stong rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/gzhan yang dud 'gro rnams kyi lus la zho dang sbrang rtsi sbags la nyin re bzhin sbyin sreg byas na ra lug la 
[\[103a.4\]]sogs pa rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/ba lang gi lhas kyi nang du ku sha'i me tog mar dang sbrang rtsis byugs nas 'bum tsho gcig sbyin sreg byas na 'byung po dang /_sha za dbang du 'gyur ro/_/rig sngags thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro/_/ji ltar 'dod pa rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/
[\[103a.5\]]yang ba lang gi lhas kyi nang du 'o ma dang 'o thug za zhing /_shri ri pa la'i yam shing la sbyin sreg 'bum byas na gang 'dod pa'i don gsol ba btab pa de rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/mtshan mo gsum du smyung bar gnas la zla ba'am/_nyi ma gzas bzung ba la ldong ros dang gi 
[\[103a.6\]]wang srang lngas a shwat+tha'i 'dab ma bzhi la g.yas skor g.yon skor du bzhag nas/_yang 'dab ma bzhis g.yogs la ji srid dro bar gyur pa de srid du bzlas pa bya'o/_/du ba dang 'bar bas 'di ltar sa bla sa 'og sa stengs gsum 'grub par 'gyur ro/_/ba lang gi lhas 
[\[103a.7\]]kyi nang ngam chu bo 'dus par/_bsod snyoms za ba'am 'o thug za bas/_arga'i 'o thug mar dang sbrang rtsis byugs nas stong tsho lnga sbyin sreg byas na rang nyid kyis nor gyi bdag po nor bu bzang po nor gyi bdag po nor dang bcas pa mthong bar 'gyur ro/_/nga mgu'o zhes 
[\[103b\]]
[\[103b.1\]]de smra na/_mchog brgyad gang 'dod pa ster bar 'gyur te/_rgyal po dang /_gter dang /_rdzu 'phrul gyis 'chag pa dang /_rig pa 'dzin pa dang /_thams cad dbang du byed pa dang /_klu dang /_gnod sbyin dang /_srin po dang /_'byung po dang /_sha za dang /_grul 
[\[103b.2\]]bum dang /_lus srul po rnams thams cad dbang du 'gyur ro/_/dran pa tsam gyis mdun du 'dug par 'gyur ro/_/rkang bzhi pa la sogs pa'i sems can shi ba rab tu zhi bar byed pa dang /_sa 'og tu 'jug pa dang /_nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang /_sa 'og gi 
[\[103b.3\]]'khrul 'khor rab tu 'jig pa dang /_chu rengs pa dang /_bcud len dang /_tshar bcad pa dang /_rjes su gzung ba brgyad po 'di rnams las de'i mdun du gang na gang gcig blang bar bya'o/_/des gang ci 'dod pa de ster bar 'gyur ro/_/pad+ma mar dang 
[\[103b.4\]]sbrang rtsis byugs nas 'bum du sbyin sreg byas na/_pad+ma rA ga'i nor bu rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/de ltar ut+pa la sngon po dang /_ku mu da rnams dri zhim po dang ldan pas kha dog sna tshogs pa'i nor bu rin po che rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/yungs kar dkar po mar dang sbrang rtsis byugs la 
[\[103b.5\]]gang gi ming nas bzung nas sbyin sreg byas na mtshan mo bdun gyis dbang du 'gyur ro/_/til nag po la mar dang sbrang rtsis sba gsal 'bum du sbyin sreg byas na nor nye bar 'phel bar 'gyur ro/_/a rga'i shing la me btang la stong phrag brgyad du sbyin sreg byas na/_nyi ma 
[\[103b.6\]]bdun gyis nad zhi bar 'gyur ro/_/dkar po'i tshes gcig nas brtsams nas sha ta puSh+pa dang /_kun da dang /_ta ka ra dang /_ba sha ke dang /_du ru ska dang /_gu gul rnams ji ltar 'tshong ba nyos la/_mchod pa byas nas mar dang sbrang rtsis sbags la/_stong phrag 
[\[103b.7\]]brgyad du sbyin sreg byas na/_nyi ma bdun du bdun 'gyur gyi nor rnyed par 'gyur ro/_/'bum phrag bzhi bzlas na/_bdag dang gzhan nye bar 'gyur bar byed do/_/yul srung bar 'gyur ro/_/na mo rat+na tra yA ya/_na mo ma Ni b+ha drA ya/_ma hA yak+Sha se nA pa ta ye/_
[\[104a\]]
[\[104a.1\]]ki Ni ki Ni g+haN+Ta ka r+Na swa ba naM me d+ha ras ma ye swA hA/_arga'i mar khus ku mu da'i me tog sbyin sreg byas na/_rmi lam yang dag pa ci lta ba bzhin mthong bar 'gyur ro/_/ki Ni ki Ni g+han Da ka r+Na tsi tra me d+ha ra yA ya swA hA/_don nges pa 
[\[104a.2\]]ster na cho ga ji ltar brjod pa bzhin no/_/'phags pa gnod gnas kyi dbang po ji ltar 'byung ba'i rtog pa zhes bya ba rdzogs [{]s+ho[,]so[}]//_//rgya gar gyi mkhan po sgeg pa'i rdo rje dang /_bod kyi lots+tsha ba dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa rdo rje grags kyis 
[\[104a.3\]]bsgyur ba'o//_//[{D771}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_/Ar+ya dzam+b+ha la nA ma aSh+Ta sha ta ka_/bod skad du/_'phags pa gnod 'dzin gyi mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa zhes bya ba/_'phags pa gnod 'dzin la 
[\[104a.4\]]phyag 'tshal lo/_/de nas gnod sbyin 'brog gnas po/_/gser dag gis ni legs par brgyan/_/rin chen gyis ni rab mdzes shing /_/me ni rab tu 'bar 'dra ba/_/lcang lo can du zhugs nas kyang /_/gsang bdag rdo rje 'chang ba yi/_/zhabs gnyis la ni 
[\[104a.5\]]rab 'jus nas/_/shin tu mnyam gzhag dris pa ni/_/bcom ldan gnod 'dzin rgyal dbang po/_/gsang sngags tshogs ni kun gyi bdag_/rig sngags 'chang rnams kun gyis mchod/_/lha dang lha min phyag byas pa/_/ma rungs 'dul la brtson pa po/_/byang chub 
[\[104a.6\]]sems dpa'i yon tan ldan/_/mgon po sems can kun don mdzad/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba 'dzin/_/sems can rnams la phan 'dod pas/_snying rjes non pa'i yid kyis su/_/yang dag rdzogs pa'i byang chub phyir/_/bdag gis kyang ni sems bskyed de/_/
[\[104a.7\]]mi rnams nor ni nyung ba dang /_/bsod nams chung zhing dbang chung ba/_/mthong nas sdug bsngal chen po yis/_/rab tu gzir to gsang ba'i bdag_/de nas gnod 'dzin gyis smras nas/_/bcom ldan gsang ba gsang ba'i bdag_/snying rjes non te smras pa ni/_/
[\[104b\]]
[\[104b.1\]]legs par nyon cig gsang ba pa/_/mgon po gnod 'dzin dpal dang ldan/_/sems can kun gyi don byed pa/_/dbul ba'i nyon mongs sel ba bo/_/nor ro cog gi dbang phyug gi/_/mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad bsod nams ldan/_/dbul ba'i nyes sdig sel byed pa/_/
[\[104b.2\]]gang gA'i bye ma'i grangs snyed kyis/_/rgyal mchog rnams kyis sngon gsungs pa/_/'od zer brgya pa zhes pa yi/_/zhing na sangs rgyas nyi ma'i zhal/_/chos ston pa na bdag gis kyang /_/de ni rang gis sngon thos te/_/dbul ba sel cing bsod nams ldan/_/de ni bdag 
[\[104b.3\]]gi shes rab kyis/_/sems can kun don brtson pa po/_/khyod la legs par bstan par bya/_/khyod ni mnyam gzhag rab tu nyon/_/'phags pa lha dang lha min bla/_/shes rab ldan zhing chos la gus/_/snying brtse'i bdag nyid bzod ldan brtan/_/dbang po zhi ba 
[\[104b.4\]]dbang po thul/_/dge bas sdig 'joms shes nyen can/_/des shing don kun sgrub pa po/_/mi gnod mi slu dpal dang ldan/_/mdzod bdag gzhan gyis mi thub pa/_/dkon mchog gsum gyi skyabs gcig pa/_/sangs rgyas kun gyis gzigs pa po/_/gter rnams 
[\[104b.5\]]skyong ba gzi brjid can/_/rtag sbyin nor ni 'phel byed pa/_/rin chen 'byung gnas skye bo 'dul/_/chu yi bdag po chu 'bebs pa/_/gnod sbyin chu spyod bdag nyid can/_/gter don nye bar ston pa po/_/gser gyi ri bo lhun po ste/_/dbul ba'i gdon las thar byed pa/_/
[\[104b.6\]]dbang po nye dbang 'gro ba'i mgon/_/chu yi dbang po sprin mdog can/_/'jig rten mig dang 'jig rten bla/_/nyi ma zla ba ther zug pa/_/nor chen rgyal po chen po ste/_/lag na ne'u le rab gnas pa/_/gzhon nu seng ge tog can te/_/gnod sbyin chen po rdzu 'phrul che/_/tshig 
[\[104b.7\]]gi bdag po bzhin 'dzum pa/_/gsong por snyan par smra ba bo/_/bram ze 'dod pa'i lcags kyu ste/_/che ba don grub grub pas mchod/_/rig sngags 'chang ba 'khor los sgyur/_/ku be ra dang mi la zhon/_/bum pa'i lto can mig yangs pa/_/lha yi dri ldan yid ltar 
[\[105a\]]
[\[105a.1\]]mgyogs/_/khyab bdag bde 'byung nor bzang sras/_/sems can rnams ni skyong la dga'/_/'dod dgur bsgyur gzugs yid kyi lha/_/cod pan can de rigs dga' ba/_/g.yon phyogs cod pan lag na dbyug_/lag pa brgya pa stobs po che/_/sa 
[\[105a.2\]]brgyad dbang phyug lha yul ba/_/zla ba nya ba'i zhal mdog can/_/ded dpon tshogs kyi bdag po ste/_/gnas brtan tshong ba skal bzang ba/_/yid bzhin nor bu bum pa bzang /_/dpag bsam ljon shing mi yi bdag_/mchog don 'os pa gtso bo ste/_/mchog sbyin 
[\[105a.3\]]mi'u thung khyab 'jug pa/_/skyabs 'os bkra shis srung ba bo/_/rin chen phreng bas rnam par brgyan/_/lha yi seng ge'i khri la bzhugs/_/byang chub sems dpa' dpal gyi bdag_/rab tu dar ba nor mi zad/_/seng ge'i rtsal gyi mthu rtsal can/_/ston pa 'jig 
[\[105a.4\]]rten gsum las rgyal/_/gtso bo tshong pa rigs kyi mchog_/pad+ma'i lte ba thub med rgyal/_/tshangs par spyod pa rgya mtsho che/_/gnod 'dzin bdag nyid che ba yi/_/ming brgya rtsa brgya dang sa bshad 'di/_/sdig pa thams cad 'joms byed cing /_/dbul ba'i nyon 
[\[105a.5\]]mongs sel byed pa/_/'byor dang skal bzang skyed pa po/_/glang po rta nor 'phel byed pa/_/gza' dang rgyu skar rmi lam ngan/_/ltas ngan sel bar byed pa ste/_/nags sam gal te grong dang ni/_/dur khrod yang na ri yang rung /_/mkhas pa gang na klog pa der/_/
[\[105a.6\]]g.yul dang dgra ni nyam nga ba/_/sbrul dang me chu chom rkun sogs/_/stag dang dom dang 'jigs pa che/_/rgya mtsho bgrod dka' mi bzad las/_/mi ni rab tu zhi bar 'gyur/_/dbang po me dang chu lha dang /_/gshin rje srin bdag rlung lha dang /_/nor sbyin dpal 
[\[105a.7\]]ldan su be ra/_/nor bu bzang sras lngas rtsen dang /_/rtsed mo can dang 'brog gnas dang /_/lha dang gnod sbyin gzhan dag kyang /_/g.yel ba med par nyin mtshan du/_/rab tu dga' bzhin srung bar byed/_/gang na ming 'di klog pa der/_/glang chen rta dang ba lang dang /_/lo tog rnam pa sna 
[\[105b\]]
[\[105b.1\]]tshogs dang /_/'bras bu me tog rnams kyang 'phel/_/mi nad dang ni 'go ba'i nad/_/gnod pa kun las byung ba rnams/_/thams cad du ni bde legs 'gyur/_/lhag par byis pa rnams la shis/_/de la [{]yi dgas [,]yi dwags [}]klu rnams dang /_/ma mo dang ni gdon drag dang /_/mkha' 'gro ma dang mi'am 
[\[105b.2\]]ci/_/srin po rnams kyang 'tshe mi byed/_/nad do cog las rnam par grol/_/de bzhin bde zhing nor dang ldan/_/bu dag dang ni tsha bo dang /_/dpal dang gtong ba rnams kyis rgyas/_/rigs mchog rgyal ba 'byung ba dang /_/longs spyod chen po'i nang du skye/_/tshe dang dpal dang ldan pa dang /_/

[\[130a.3\]]zhus pa'i le'u drug pa'o//_//mi gang mi yi sha ni 'tshong 'dod des/_/mar gyi ngo la dur khrod song nas su/_/shing rdo mtshon dang dug dang dbyug to sman/_/bgegs la sogs pas shi bar gyur pa yi/_/byin pa brla dang ske dang mgo bo dag_/'jigs pa med pas mtshan 
[\[130a.4\]]mo blangs nas su/_/gtubs te kong bu'am gyo dum gsar pa dang /_gtsang ma der ni mi nyung bzhag byas la/_/lus la khrag gi lag rjes bris nas su/_/rgyu mas mgo dang mgrin pa dkri bar bya/_/lus la mi sbags sar pa bgos nas kyang /_/lag g.yon shas bkang gyo mo 
[\[130a.5\]]thogs nas su/_/khrag gis bskus pa'i ral gri lag g.yas kyis/_/rab tu bsgrims nas de ni thogs nas kyang /_/sgra cher bod cing tshig tu sha 'di dag_/khyed cag su zhig nyo bar byed 'dod ces/_/shar dang nub dang lho dang byang phyogs su/_/myur du bskor cing shin tu brjod par 
[\[130a.6\]]bya/_/ci ste lus ni snang ngam mi snang bar/_/tshig gis khyod ni nor ram rig pa'am/_/bcud kyis len pa'am grong ngam rgyal srid dam/_/phug tu 'gro ba'am ci 'dod ces zer na/_/sngar ni gang zhig sems kyis bsams pa'i don/_/de nyid smra yi gzhan ni smra mi bya/_/rig pa mang 
[\[130a.7\]]po bsten pa'i dur khrod 'dir/_/don 'di'i phyir ni sdug bsngal drag po yis/_/bdag kyang gdungs bzhin 'ongs kyis 'di nyid na/_/yod na sha 'di khyer la bdag la byin/_/ci ste srang la bcal te ma gang na/_/rang gi sha yis de ni dgang bar bya/_/gal te dur khrod 'di ni 
[\[130b\]]
[\[130b.1\]]stong pa ste/_/nor med bu khyod gzhan du song shig ces/_/mtshan mo rgyu bas de skad bsgo na ni/_/de la bdag ni gang du 'gro zhes dri/_/lan thob de nyid rang gis brtags nas su/_/sha de bor nas de nas 'gro bar bya/_/sha yi cho ga gang zhig ngas gsungs pa/_/
[\[130b.2\]]gsang sngags ma bzlas pa yis bsten mi bya/_/rigs mchog gtsug tor stobs chen la sogs pas/_/dur khrod du ni bsrung ba rangs gsungs so/_/gsang sngags drag po gang zhig sha za ba/_/de la dur khrod mi sha'i sbyin sreg bya/_/ral gris sor gnyis sor gsum tsam 
[\[130b.3\]]dag tu/_/gtubs nas me la sbyin sreg stong du bya/_/me tog mnyams 'bras yos sha khrag nya/_/chang dang sbrang rtsi bu ra ma chang dang til/_/bdug pa phreng ba byug pa mar me chan/_/lha bshos gtor ma dur khrod gtor bar bya/_/dbab dang bskrad dang gnyid kyis myos bya dang /_/
[\[130b.4\]]dmag gzhom grong khyer phung bar bya ba dang /_/sha za ma mo drag mo srin mo'i tshogs/_/gnod sbyin rnams la mi sha'i sbyin sreg bya/_/mi yi sha ni rnyed par ma gyur na/_/ba glang sha yi sbyin sreg de bzhin shis/_/ma he'i sha 'am khyi sha mar bsres la/_/tshes grangs dag la smyung byas sbyin 
[\[130b.5\]]sreg bya/_/gnod sbyin mo ya cho ga zhib mor ni/_/gsang sngags mnyes byas grub pa 'di rnams ster/_/ma dang sgyug mo sru mo grogs mo dang /_/bu mo chung ma mna' mar grub par 'gyur/_/ma dang sgyug mo sru mo gang yin de/_/yid bzhin rin chen bzhin du grub pa mchog_/yid 
[\[130b.6\]]'ong grogs mo bu mo grub pa 'bring /_/chung ma mna' ma grub pa tha mar bsgrags/_/dus gsum du ni me tog phreng ba dri/_/mar ram 'bru mar mar me tsan+dan dang /_/a kar dri zhim bdug pas mchod pa dang /_/gtor ma sna tshogs rtag tu mtshan mo sbyin/_/gnod sbyin mo ni dga' 
[\[130b.7\]]nas mngon phyogs nas/_/rnyed pa rnyed cing sa bon 'byung bar byed/_/'dod chags zil gyis non pa'i bud med dag_/gnod pa byed pa nges par gnas par 'gyur/_/bsams na phung bar yang ni 'gyur ba nyid/_/bud med gnod pa byed tshe 'gro mi bya/_/rnyed pa mang nyung la yang 
[\[131a\]]
[\[131a.1\]]'dod mi skyed/_/sngags pas mtshan mo khu ba dgag byas nas/_/brtson 'grus rab tu bskyed de bsgrub par bya/_/sems rmongs gang gis gzhan du brtsam byas na/_/gnod sbyin mos ni myur du phung bar byed/_/sha za'i gnod sbyin ma la'ang de nyid de/_/de las 
[\[131a.2\]]cho ga lhag pa 'di rnams bya/_/sha chang la phug tshod ma cung peng dang /_/nas cha nam sha chan dang 'bras chan nya/_/gtor ma de dag kun du bdug pa dbul/_/gnas ni kha stong dag gam dur khrod shis/_/me tog shir sha kun dur arka dang /_/bil ba 'bri ha ku sha ra rdza ka_/a 
[\[131a.3\]]gas ut+pal a ta ru sha ka_/se'u can mya ngan tshang sogs me tog dbul/_/klu la bu ra ma 'o ma mar sbyar ba'i/_/bdug pa dri zhim a kar tsan+dan dri/_/phreng ba me tog dri zhim sna tshogs dang /_/'bras chan zho dang 'bras yos 'bras bu dbul/_/ba dan sngon po bum pa sngon po 
[\[131a.4\]]dang /_/gos kyang sngon po lha bshos gtor ma dri/_/phreng ba me tog byug pa sngon po dag_/ci snyed brang gis 'gro ba rnams la dbul/_/mthe bong me long ral gri chu dang shel/_/mar me sa gzhi lcags dang nam mkha' dang /_/lhung bzed nor bu dag dang me 'bar ba/_/'di la 
[\[131a.5\]]gsal bar ston pa rtag tu 'byung /_/'das pa dang ni ma 'ongs da ltar byung /_/mtho ris sa steng dus dang mi ldan yang /_/lha dang lha min dge dang mi dge ba'i/_/las rnams thams cad gsal bar ston par rtogs/_/cho ga nyams pa'am yang na phyed bzlas pa'am/_/yi ge 
[\[131a.6\]]chad dam yi ge lhag pa'am/_/bzlas brjod ma byas dad pa med pa dang /_/mchod pa med cing sa gzhi mi gtsang dang /_/sprin gyi tshogs kyis nyi zer bsgribs pa dang /_/byis pa yan lag nyams shing lhag pa dang /_/de lta bu la mi yi gsal ston pa/_/'bab par mi 'gyur dgos 
[\[131a.7\]]pa yong mi ston/_/gsal ston dbab phyir sngon du cho ga bzhin/_/bzlas shing tshes grangs bzang la sngags pa yang /_/smyung byas dgongs kar sa dang lci ba yis/_/ba ko tsam gyis sa gzhi legs par byug_/byug spos dang ni me tog bdug spos dang /_/lha bshos mar me dag 
[\[131b\]]
[\[131b.1\]]kyang phul nas su/_/byis pa gzhon nu sta gon gnas par bya/_/de nas nang par cho ga 'di kun bya/_/khrus byas lus la gos dkar gtsang bgos te/_/shar phyogs kha bltas ku sha'i stan steng du/_/'dug nas gsang sngags rjes su dran par bya/_/me long thal ba gtsang 
[\[131b.2\]]mas lan bdun nam/_/brgyad dam yang na bcur ni phyis nas su/_/rtse gcig sems kyis gsang sngags zlos bzhin du/_/bus pa gzhon nu nub tu kha bstan nas/_/lha yi mig gis bltas na 'das pa dang /_/da ltar dang ni ma 'ongs mthong bar 'gyur/_/me long zhes bya'i cho 
[\[131b.3\]]ga mtha' dag ni/_/ral gri gsal bar ston la sbyar bar bya/_/mthe bo rgya skyegs khu bas bskus nas su/_/'bru mar dri zhim dag gis bsku bar bya/_/bum pa gtsang ma chus bkang mi g.yor bzhag_/sa bcags lhung bzed nor bu chu yis dgang /_/sku gzugs la ni byug 
[\[131b.4\]]spos me tog dbul/_/de nas bu sa pa gzhon nus blta bar bya/_/gsal bar ston dang rmi lam la sogs pas/_/dngos grub brtags te de nas bzlas brjod bya/_/gal te yid ches par ni ma gyur na/_/de nas rig sngags mi gdug bzlas brjod bya/_/nga yi gsang sngags dag pa gang 
[\[131b.5\]]yang rung /_/gso sbyong byas nas nan tan bzung nas su/_/rgyal ba'i ring bsrel mchod rten drung du bzlas/_/yang na sku gzugs mnyams spyan sngar bzlas/_/lus dang ngag yid lag pa mig dang ni/_/smin mtshams yan lag rnam par g.yo ba dag_/rab tu bsdams nas de la 
[\[131b.6\]]yid gzhol zhing /_/byams la gnas shing ku sha'i khres la 'dug_/ji srid du ni rtse gcig gnas 'gyur pa/_/de srid bar du 'bum mam nyis 'bum bzlas/_/nga yi gsang sngags hu~M zhes bya ba 'dis/_/shing la'ang 'bab na mi la smos ci dgos/_/de nas dbab pa'i snod rnams brtag 
[\[131b.7\]]par bya/_/bu mo gzhon nu lo bcu 'am bcu gnyis pa/_/bcu 'am brgyad dam bdun nam bzhi 'am gsum/_/yang na khye'u'ang rung ste gnyis sam lnga/_/tshigs rus rtsa mi mngon zhing gzugs bzang ba/_/yan lag rdzogs shing mig da kyus ring la dkar/_/kha bzhin zla 'dra mche ba mnyam 
[\[132a\]]
[\[132a.1\]]la rno/_/sor mo thags bzang mdzes la long bu nub/_/lte ba zab cing mdzes la nu mjing legs/_/ba spu re re skra yang gnag la stug_/lto ba mi 'o gnyer ma gsum dang ldan/_/mdog kyang bzang zhing mnga' byad dang yang ldan/_/gang la yid dga' lta ba

[\[132a.3\]]la sogs gtor ma mang /_/lha dang lha min gnod sbyin rnams la sbyin/_/dbab pa'i snod rnams khrus byas gos dkar bskon/_/shar phyogs kha bltas rgyan ni rnam par spangs/_/byug spos me tog la sogs de la sbyin/_/bdug pas bdug cing gsang sngags bzlas brjod bya/_/
[\[132a.4\]]hU~M gi gsang sngags thog mar bzlas nas su/_/grih+Na a be sha zhes brjod par bya/_/mig ni gdang sa shing 'dzums par mi byed na/_/rdzogs par gyur par shes par byas nas su/_/'jigs pa med par de tshe dri bya ba/_/mchod yon dang ni bdug pa phul nas su/_/rig pa mchog 
[\[132a.5\]]gi gsang sngags dran byas nas/_/phyag 'tshal nas ni lha phyogs gang yin dri/_/dus gsum dag gi bdag gi dgos pa gang /_/de ni legs par dgongs la bka' stsol cig_/_bde dang sdug bsngal dngos grub thob mi thob/_/shes nas de yang de bzhin bzung nas su/_/de ma thag 
[\[132a.6\]]tu slar yang gtang bar bya/_/mi gdug sngags bzlas cho ga 'di rnams kyis/_/dbab pa'i snod la mi yis phebs gyur gyi/_/gang zhig blun pas gzhan du brtsams na ni/_/de ni mi rnams kun gyis dpyas par 'gyur/_/zhi zhing gzhungs la rgya che da kyus kyang ring /_/brtan zhing gzi 
[\[132a.7\]]chen mdangs ldan dmar bar snang /_/'dzums zhing 'byed med lha yi mig dang 'dra/_/dbab pa'i snod la lha babs de ltar 'gyur/_/mig ni rab tu dmar zhing zlum por 'dug_/bgrad cing rab tu mi sdug 'jigs 'jigs lta/_/'dzums pa med cing 'jigs med blta ba na/_/srin 
[\[132b\]]
[\[132b.1\]]po lto 'phye gnod sbyin babs pa'i mig_/gal te babs pa'i snod ni mi gtong na/_/shin tu bkra shis tshigs bcad brjod pa'am/_/stobs po che'am dgod ma'am lcags kyu bzlas/_/yang na rab tu 'dus pa'i mdo sde bklag_/seng ge gdan gyi arka'am pa la sha'i/_/
[\[132b.2\]]yam shing mar gyis bskus pa brgya yang bsreg_/ma grugs til ni sbrang rtsi 'am mar gyis bskus/_/gtum pos sbyin sreg nyi shu rtsa gcig bya/_/snga ma bzhin du gsang sngags cho ga dag_/dam tshig ci bzhin ma lus sbyar na ni/_/bdag gi yid dang mthun pa'i dngos grub

[\[132b.5\]]kyis/_/gus par dge ba'i bsod nams gang bsags pa'ang /_/bde gshegs gsungs pa'i bden pa'i la ma dmigs na/_/dge ba'i lam de yang dag bskyed pa yin/_/yongs su 'dzin pa rnam par spangs nas su/_/chos gos dang ni bsod snyoms ngan ngon dang /_/sman dang mal 
[\[132b.6\]]stan ngan ngon tsam gyis kyang /_/chog pa'i sems dang ldan pas bsod nams thob/_/bdag la bstod pa na mas kyang mi bya zhing /_/sems can gzhan la smad par mi bya'o/_/stag dang sbrul dang me 'drar 'jig rten dag_/bsams nas spangs te dben la dga' bar bya/_/bud med

[\[133a\]]
[\[133a.1\]]mo byis par lug sogs/_/thab mo 'gyed pa mi blta mi bya'o/_/yul sa'i gtam dang mi dbang bstan pa dang /_/dmag dang gyad dang na chung gtam dag dang /_/sgrung ldebs dang ni sngon gyi lo rgyus gtam/_/'dod chags dang ni smad 'tshong gtam mi bya/_/
[\[133a.2\]]sngags pa gsang sngags bzlas pa mnos pa ni/_/grong dang grong khyer khyim dang gtsug lag khang /_/mchod rten bsti gnas ri dang dka' thub gnas/_/kun dga' lu ma'am rdzing bur 'gro mi bya/_/sngar bshad pa yi gnas rnams ma rnyed na/_/lha khang stong pa dag gam shing drung 
[\[133a.3\]]ngam/_/ri dang chu bo chu klung 'bab chu dang /_/nags tshal stong pa dang ni yul stong dang /_/gnas gang rung bar sngags pas gnas shing bzlas/_/yang na gnas ni nges par ma byas na/_/zla ba brgyad po 'di yi dus dag tu/_/gnas 'di gang yang rung ba zhig tu bsten/_/mtsho dang shing dang 
[\[133a.4\]]ri bo'am dgon pa'i gnas/_/mtshe'u dang khang pa gnas sam chu ngogs su/_/dgun dpyid zla ba rnams la gnas byas nas/_/sngags pas dbyaro ni gcig tu gnas byas te/_/ci ltar rgyal bas dge slong dbyar zla gsum/_/tshul zhugs gnas gzhan mi 'gror gsungs pa 
[\[133a.5\]]bzhin/_/de bzhin bcom ldan 'das kyis bsngags pa yang /_/zla ba gsum du gcig tu gnas par gsungs/_/sngags pas dbyar ni ba sgrub la mi 'jug par/_/bzlas brjod kyis ni dus kyang 'das par bya/_/dbyar 'das dang ni gsang sngags gzi bskyed pas/_/bdag nyid 
[\[133a.6\]]bsrung byas bsgrub la 'jug par bya/_/me thab zlum po gru gsum gru bzhi dang /_/pad+ma lta bur bya zhing dbyibs legs shing /_/'jam zhing shin tu mnyam par byas nas su/_/de dag sa dang lci bas legs par byug_/zlum po dbang thang bskyed dang nor dgug dang /_/spyan drang 
[\[133a.7\]]zhi ba'i cho ga bya bar shis/_/gru gsum du ni dgar bskrad bsad pa dang /_/gshed byed la sogs drag po'i las kyang bya/_/gru bzhi par ni klu dang gsang ba pa'i/_/srog bskam pa'am yan lag gzhig par bya/_/pad+ma'i dbyibs su bud med bu mo'i grong /_/yul 'khor 'thob 
[\[133b\]]
[\[133b.1\]]pa'am don kun bsgrub par shis/_/me thab lci ba gtsang mas byugs nas kyang /_/tha ma thog tog ku sha dgram par bya/_/dkon mchog gsum dang phyag na rdo rje dang /_/yum la'ang dad pas phreng ba bdug pa dang /_/dri dang mnyams me tog ci snyed pas/_/cho ga bzhin 
[\[133b.2\]]du legs par mchod par bya/_/yam shing mang po thab kyi drung bzhag ste/_/rlung yab kyis ni me yang spar byas nas/_/sangs rgyas rnams la phyag byas khro bo ni/_/bdud rtsi 'khyil pas mnyams pad+ma 'am/_/ma grugs til nag las ni bdun nam brgya da/_/bcu 'am nyi 
[\[133b.3\]]shur bsreg blugs me la bsreg_/ku sha bting ngam khres sam rtswa stan la/_/'dug nas shar phyogs kha bstan rdzas rnams ni/_/mar dang sbrang rtsi 'o ma la btags nas/_/rang gi gsang sngags bsgrub phyir sbyin sreg bya/_/me yi mtshan ma nye bar brtag pa ni/_/me stag 
[\[133b.4\]]du ba me lce sgra rnams la sa/_/grub pa dang ni mi grub thams cad kyang /_/sngags kyis byin brlabs me ni ston par byed/_/du ba med cing gser gyi mdog ltar dang sa/_/me lce rab tu che la g.yas su 'khyil/_/kha dog 'ja' 'dra yang na dkar yang rung /_/yang na byi ru ba cag 
[\[133b.5\]]pa'i kha dog 'dra/_/shin tu snum la me lce sgab nas 'phro/_/rab tu 'bar ba nyi ma'i 'od zer 'dra/_/dbyibs ni bum pa rgyal mtshan gdugs kyang 'dra/_/dpal be'u dang ni pad+ma blugs gzar 'dra/_/me lce tri shul rdo rje ral gri 'dra/_/yang na shing rta mchog dang rnga yab 'dra/_/rdza 
[\[133b.6\]]rnga rnga chen dang ni gling bu'i sgra/_/du ba me lce dri zhim me stag bzang /_/yang nam spar bar ni 'bar 'gyur na/_/de tshe dngos grub rgya chen thob par 'gyur/_/dud pa che zhing me stag rgod pa dang /_/'bar bar dka' zhing cung zad cung zad 'bar/_/me lce rnam par chad cing gzi mdangs 
[\[133b.7\]]med/_/rtsub gnag sprin dang pa la sha yi mdog_/gsal shing 'dra zhing zhib ma'i gzugs kyang 'dra/_/phyugs kyi mgo 'dra skra yang rab tu rtsub/_/me lce 'phro bas sbyin sreg byed pa tshig_/mi ro'i dri nga dngos grub med pa ston/_/me lce'i mtshan ma 'di 'dra mthong nas kyang /_/stobs 
[\[134a\]]
[\[134a.1\]]po che yi mar gyis sbyin sreg bya/_/byin pa dag dang mchan khung spu rnams ni/_/lag pas kyang ni btog par mi bya zhing /_/me yas mi bsreg spu gris brag mi bya/_/spu med bya phyir sman gyis mi byug go/_/ji ltar ral gri so la 'dzin pa'i mis/_/legs

[\[134a.3\]]yi glags mthong nas nas ni phung bar byed/_/ba sgrub pa kun la dang po kho nar ni/_/lha bshos gtor ma phal cher dbul bar bya/_/sngags pa'i las grub nas kyang dus kun du/_/rang gi nyams kyis ci snyed dbul bar bya/_/lha dang lha min gnod sbyin lto 'phye grul/_/nam mkha'

[\[134a.5\]]gnas nas phan gdags phyir ni 'dir spyon cig_/'byung po gang dag ri rab steng gnas dang /_/dga' ba'i tshal dang lha yi gnas rnams dang /_/shar nub ri dang nyi zla'i khyim rnams dang /_/ri bo kun la gang dag gnas pa dang /_/chu bo kun dang chu yi mdo rnams dang /_/rin chen 
[\[134a.6\]]gnas na lhag par gang gnas dang /_/mtsho dang rdzing dang lteng ka chu ngogs dang /_/g.ya' chu sil ma can na gang gnas dang /_/grong dang phyugs lhas grong khyer stong pa'am/_/khang stong dang ni lha yi khang pa dang /_/gtsug lag khang dang mchod rten gnas dag gam/_/dka' 
[\[134a.7\]]thub gnas sam glang chen bres dag gam/_/rgyal po'i da kor khang dag na gang gnas dang /_/lam srang 'dun sa dang ni bzhi mdo dang /_/gang dag lam po che dang shing gcig dang /_/dur khrod chen po'am nags tshal chan po dang /_/seng ge dred dang ga can gzan gnas dag 
[\[134b\]]
[\[134b.1\]]dang /_/'brog chen 'jigs su rung bar gang gnas dang /_/gang dag gling mchog rnams na gnas pa dang /_/lhun po dur khrod dag na gnas pa rnams/_/rab tu dgyes shing mgu bar gyur nas su/_/phreng ba me tog dri dang bdug pa dang /_/bstod dang gtor ma mar me

[\[134b.4\]]gtor ma phul ba rnams/_/rab tu dgyes pa yis ni bzhes nas kyang /_/rang rang phyogs su legs par bzhugs nas su/_/rang gi bu smad mdza' bshes gnyen 'dun dang /_/nang mi dpung bcas dmag dang thabs cig tu/_/me tog dri dang gtor ma byug par bcas/_/
[\[134b.5\]]'di rnams btung zhing legs par gsol nas kyang /_/bdag gi las 'di'i 'bras bu mchis par mdzod/_/de ltar gang zhig mtshan mo rgyu ba la/_/gtor ma gtong ba'i las rnams byed pa de'i/_/dngos grub myur zhing shin tu bgegs kyang med/_/yid du 'ong ba'i 'dod

[\[135a\]]
[\[135a.1\]]mongs zad pa'i ma ni sun 'byin dang /_/slob pa gsod cing dge 'dun mnga' ba la/_/gang zhig 'dod pas mang nyung rku 'phrog pa/_/mtshams med nye lngar de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs/_/tshul nyams mi ni gang zhig 'di byed pa/_/bskal pa'i bar du mnar 
[\[135a.2\]]med sdug bsngal myong /_/gsang sngags dngos grub bsgrims kyang yong mi thob/_/gang zhig bde gshegs gsung gi glegs bam dag_/chud gson pa dang mes ni sreg pa dang /_/bsam pa ngan pas chur ni 'dor ba dang /_/yang na chos kyi sku ni spong ba'am/_/bslab tshig ma lus

[\[135b\]]
[\[135b.1\]]dge 'dun la ni mi gus pa/_/'byung por byin pa'am lha yi gtor ma 'am/_/sa la lhung ba sngags pas bza' mi bya/_/'dod chags zil gyis gnon pa'i dud 'gro dang /_/bud med bgrod bya min par 'gro mi bya/_/glang chen mi gdul sbrul yang mi gzung zhing /_/rta rgyug glo 
[\[135b.2\]]rdebs lcag gis gzhu mi bya/_/las de rnams dang ldan par gyur pa de'i/_/dngos grub nam yang 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro/_/sems can nad kyis gdungs dang sdug bsngal la/_/rtag tu byams pa yang ni yid la bya/_/dper na nam mkha' mtha' thug med pa la/_/'dom gyis

[\[136a\]]
[\[136a.1\]]phyag mi bya/_/skyes bu bsam yas rmad byung rdzu 'phrul can/_/de la mi ngan gang zhig mi 'dud pa/_/de la rgyal ba thams cad thugs nur nas/_/de yi gsang sngags dngos grub mi stsol lo/_/dper na shing gi me tog dang por ni/_/yid 'ong phyi nas 'bras

[\[136a.5\]]ba'i phyir/_/dkyil 'khor bcas shing phyag rgyar ldan pa yi/_/gsang sngags bye ba phrag bdun rab tu bshad/_/pho nya bcu dang rig pa'i rgyal po bdun/_/de bzhin phyag brnyan drug cu rtsa bzhi dang /_/nga yi snying po dam pa brgyad rnams dang /_/khro bo drag po bdud rtsi thab sbyor dang /_/rig

[\[136b\]]
[\[136b.1\]]de rnams rta mgrin dkyil 'khor gsang sngags te/_/mi la mchog sbyin 'jig rten gsum gyis 'dud/_/sgral ma dkar mo gos dkar spyan ma dang /_/rnam gzigs ral pa gcig ma dkar sham dang /_/grags ldan khro gnyer can dang 'di dag rnams/_/pad+ma'i rigs kyi rig 
[\[136b.2\]]sngags rgyal mo mchog_/de dag dkyil 'khor sna tshogs gzugs can dang /_/phyag rgya rnam pa sna tshogs rnams dang ldan/_/rgyas pa'i gsang sngags rgyud du 'og pag can/_/rig pa'i dbang phyug gsang sngags bdag por bsgom/_/de ya gsang sngags mi la grub mchog ster/_/
[\[136b.3\]]de la lngas rtsen yang ni mngon par dga'/_/gnod sbyin dbang phyug de dag rtag mthun pas/_/de yi bka' yis gsang sngags tshogs rnams bshad/_/lngas rtsen gyis ni stong phrag nyi shu ste/_/de yi chung mas de yi phyed bshad do/_/nor gyi bdag pos stong phrag sum cu ste/_/
[\[136b.4\]]gang po pha yis kyang ni 'bum bshad do/_/lha dang lha min la sogs rgyal ba la/_/dad pa rnams kyis gsang sngags mtha' yas bshad/_/kha cig nga yi rigs su gtogs pa ste/_/kha cig kyang ni pad+mo'i rigs su gtogs/_/kha cig nor gyi rigs su gtogs pa yin/_/gzhan

[\[137a.1\]]grub 'dod pas gsang sngags mgo la gdon/_/bsod nams ched dang log 'dren rmongs bya'i phyir/_/phyag na rdo rje gtum mchog phyag 'tshal zhes/_/gsang sngags rnams kyi mgo la sbyar bya bar/_/gnod sbyin mgon po ngas ni bshad pa yin/_/nor

[\[138a.1\]]sngags sna tshogs gzugs su rnam sprul nas/_/gang zhig sdug bsngal gang zhig 'jigs skrag pa'am/_/rgyal po chom rkun thog gis 'jigs skrag pa'i/_/'gro ba'i tshogs chen mtha' dag skyob par mdzad/_/gang zhig yul dang khyim la bsten kyang rung /_/
[\[138a.2\]]dka' thub mnyams rtse gcig sems kyis ni/_/nyin gcig bzhin du cung zad sngags bzlas na/_/de yi gsang sngags dus shig na ni 'grub/_/cho ga bzhin du dang po 'bum bzlas nas/_/de nas sngags pa bsgrub la 'jug par bya/_/des na dngos grub myur du 'thob 'gyur 
[\[138a.3\]]la/_/gsang sngags cho gas yun ring nyon mi mongs/_/lus la sa yis dril phyis byas nas su/_/chu chen rnyog pa med par zhugs nas su/_/ci tsam 'dod pa'i bar du khrus byas te/_/byung nas shar ram byang du kha bltas nas/_/chu yis lag pa rkang pa bkrus nas su/_/pus mo phyi rol du 
[\[138a.4\]]ni bstan byas te/_/bar du lag bzhag tsog tsog por 'dug nas/_/sgra med dbu ba med pas nye reg bya/_/lan gsum bar du chu ni 'thungs nas kyang /_/mchu la lan gnyis yongs su phyi bar bya/_/so la chags pa lce yis reg pa dang /_/sbrid pa byung na kha yang bkru bar bya/_/rab byung skyes

[\[138a.7\]]dang /_/bzhon pa rgyan dang byug pa bza' btung dang /_/mal stan rnams ni mang nyung byin gyur na/_/de la bsgrub la gnas pas mi blang ngo /_/sa phung bshang sgor lnga ste mtshan la gsum/_/g.yon la gsum ste lag pa gnyis la bdun/_/yang na sa dang chu yis ci srid du/_/dri ma dri bral de srid 
[\[138b\]]
[\[138b.1\]]bar du bya/_/sos ka nags me mched pa'i me lce yis/_/ma bsgrims bzhin du tshang tshing kun bsregs ltar/_/bzlas brjod me la tshul khrims rlung gis sbar/_/brtson 'grus chen po'i me lces sdig pa sreg_/ji ltar gangs la nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis/_/gdungs na bzi brjid

[\[138b.4\]]yin de ni zad gyur na/_/des ni gsang sngags mthu yis 'di nyid du/_/mthong ba'i chos la gsang sngags 'bras bu 'thob/_/sngags kyi rtsa ba dang po tshul khrims te/_/de nas brtson 'grus dang ni bzod pa dang /_/rgyal ba la ni dad dang byang chub sems/_/gsang sngags dang ni le lo 
[\[138b.5\]]med pa'o/_/ci ltar mi dbang yan lag bdun ldan pa/_/skyo ba med par skye dgu 'dul bar byed/_/de bzhin sngags pa'ang yan lag 'di bdun dang /_/ldan na dngos grub dam pa'ang thob par 'gyur/_/dang po bzlas brjod phal cher byas nas su/_/de yi 'og tu 'dir ni sbyin sreg bya/_/
[\[138b.6\]]sbyin sreg dag gis gsang sngags mchog myur s+col/_/yid du 'ong ba'i 'dod pa'ang sbyin pa mdzad/_/gang gis dpag tshad brgya yi pha rol nas/_/gsang sngags mthu yis bud med bkug kyang ni/_/bud med ma yin gnod sbyin bu mo ste/_/de gzugs cha byad kyis ni sngags pa bstan/_/
[\[138b.7\]]'dod pa'i don phyir bsgrub pa gang yin de/_/grub na'ang gnod sbyin bu mos sbyin par byed/_/de ni bud med de ya lus su yang /_/sprul nas mtshan mo 'dod pa bsten par byed/_/ci ltar mi dag 'dod phyir bud med la/_/bsten phyir mi yi nor ni zad 'gyur ltar/_/de bzhin gnod sbyin 
[\[139a\]]
[\[139a.1\]]mo'am bran mo dag_/gsang sngags mthus bkug bsten par byed pa'o/_/gzhan gyi chung mar yid la bzhag nas su/_/gang zhig de la 'dod gdungs bsten byed pa/_/mi shes yid kyis gzhan gyi chung ma la/_/'dod pa spyad pas sdig pa mang po 'thob/_/
[\[139a.2\]]rgyal ba la dad gzhan la phan brtson pa'i/_/lha klu lha min gnod sbyin dri za dang /_/grub par bcas pa sngags bshad gang yin pa/_/de dag rgyal ba'i nyan thos rang sangs rgyas/_/de bzhin gshegs dang byang chub sems dpa' yis/_/ma 'ongs sems can mgon skyabs 
[\[139a.3\]]med rnams la/_/rab tu gzigs nas byin gyis brlab pa mdzad/_/de dag 'bras bu rab dang 'bring dang ni/_/tha mar dbye bas rnam pa gsum du bstan/_/mkha' la 'gro dang dpal gyi phug tu 'jug_/'dod dgu'i gzugs can mi snang rnam pa dang /_/gnod sbyin bu mo'i khyo dang 
[\[139a.4\]]bcud kyis len/_/mig 'phrul sgyu ma mtshan mo rgyu ba ste/_/de dag mchog yin 'bring ni sa bdag go/_/grong dang nor dang dbye dang dgug pa dang /_/dgar dang bskrad pa dang ni gsad pa dang /_/klu yi gdon gyis zin pa gso ba dang /_/gang yang 'di lta bu dang mthun pa'i las/_/de ni mkhas 
[\[139a.5\]]pas phran tshegs yin par bstan/_/bye brag tu ni klu dang gnod sbyin dang /_/byis pa gdon gyis zin dang gang dag tu/_/lus can rnams la ngo mtshar sna tshogs dag_/ston par byed pa phra mo'i phran tshegs yin/_/byab dang khu tshur thal lcag skra drang dang /_/rna bar bzlas dang dbab dang bskrad 
[\[139a.6\]]pa dang /_/gsad dang bcing la sogs pas tshar gcad dang /_/bod dang rig pa'i gos dang sngags gos dang /_/rdog pas bsnun dang rnam par bskyod pa dang /_/mig tu dug song ltar ni gzhug pa dang /_/khab kyi gzugs dang khab cing skyug tu gzhug_/_phu zhes bud dang yan lag 
[\[139a.7\]]gzhig pa dang /_/brang gis 'gro bdag kyang dgug pa dang /_/phyir yang bcing dang mnan par bya ba dang /_/rmongs dang byad dang dug zar gzhug pa dang /_/dug ni gzhan la spo bar bya ba dang /_/lcags kyur ldan pas drang bar bya ba 'am/_/lus la zhen pa'i dug ni bslang ba'am/_/zos 
[\[139b\]]
[\[139b.1\]]par bza' dang zos pa bcad pa dang /_/sa bcing ba dang pho nya gtang ba dang /_/bskrad pa dang ni klu la bstan pa dang /_/dung dang rdza rnga'i sgras ni bslang ba ste/_/rnam pa 'di dag dug gi rgyud du bshad/_/sa yi steng na sbrul ni brgyad cu dag_/gzhan la gnod par byed cing rnam par 
[\[139b.2\]]'khyam/_/de dag rnams las nyi shu gdengs ka can/_/'khyil pa drug dang dug med bcu gnyis dang /_/de bzhin sbrul ni khro bo bcu gsum ste/_/sum cu gang yin rigs de'i nang du gtogs/_/sbal pa'i mgo dang sdig pa kha brgyad dang /_/rnam par dbye na rab tu mang po yod/_/

[\[139b.5\]]gnyis kyis btab nas su/_/khrag dag byung bar gyur pa zos pa'o/_/gal te mche ba gsum gyis sha bcad na/_/de ni bcad par gyur pa yin zhes bstan/_/gang du mche ba bzhi yas btab nas su/_/sbrul gyis lus ni zos par gyur pa de/_/btab nas zas pa yin zhes bshad 
[\[139b.6\]]pa ste/_/de ni sman rnams kyis kyang bzlog par dka'/_/me ya rang bzhin gnad rnams 'dra la ba'i dug_/mtshon dang me dang gzi brjid mtshungs pa dang /_/ji ltar sngags kyis rab tu zhi 'gyur ba/_/de ltar sman pas sbyor bas mi nus so/_/ci ltar me phung chen pos bud shing la/_/

[\[140a\]]
[\[140a.1\]]ba lang khyu na seng ge ji lta bar/_/dug can sbrul dang dogs med lhan cig rtse/_/lha klu lha min gnod sbyin grub pa dang /_/dri za 'byung po mtshun dang gsang ba dang /_/[{]yi dgas [,]yi dwags [}]sha za dang ni lus srul po/_/smyo byed mdangs 'phrogs pa dang grib non dang /_/sa yi steng

[\[140b\]]
[\[140b.1\]]min gnod sbyin grub pa dang /_/rig 'dzin klu dang gnod sbyin dri za dang /_/gsang ba pa dang mtshun dang 'byung po rnams/_/dad pas zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/_/gus pas thal mo sbyar nas chig gsol pa/_/kye ma'o srog chags rnams la thugs rjer ldan/_/kye

[\[140b.3\]]dang /_/gzhan dag gis ni zhi ba nyid du mthong /_/du ma'i sku mnga' dmigs med sku mnga' bar/_/lha dang gnod sbyin gyis mchod de la 'dud/_/lha min lha yis zhabs la phyag bgyis pa/_/byang chub sems dpa' mchog la phyag 'tshal 'dud/_/rig pa'i dbang phyug gzhu 'gengs

[\[141a.1\]{D806}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_sarba maN+Dal sA mA n+ya bi d+hi na gu h+ya tan+t+ra/_bod skad du/_dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi spyi'i cho ga gsang ba'i rgyud/_thams cad mkhyen pa la phyag 'tshal lo/_/de nas gzhan yang gsang ba'i rgyud/_/dkyil 'khor dag ni thams cad

[\[141a.4\]]kun shes pa/_/tshul khrims ldan zhing snying rje'i bdag_/drang zhing bzod la gtsang sbra can/_/dad dang dran ldan snying stobs ldan/_/smra mkhas mi 'jigs sran thub pa/_/sgyu rtsal dag la mkhas shing gsal/_/mdzes dang ldan zhing de bzhin du/_/gus ldan dul la khong

[\[148b.1\]]'jig rten skyong ba la sogs pa/_/dkyil 'khor gsum pa bsdu bar bshad/_/de las gzhan rnams ji skad du/_/bshad pa de bzhin kho nar dgod/_/dkyil 'khor thig gdab thig skud ni/_/kha bsgyur gtsang ma sra zhing phra/_/de bzhin bu mo gzhon nus bkal/_/sar pa shin

[\[149a.1\]]bya/_/yid ni mos par bya ba'i phyir/_/me tog sil ma gtor bar bya/_/srad bu dag gis yongs su bskor/_/rgyal mtshan rta babs dag gis mtshan/_/brgyus pa'i phreng ba rnams bre zhing /_/bkra shis cho gar bstan par bya/_/de nas byang gi phyogs gcig

[\[153a.1\]]phyogs gsum du ni stegs bu gsum/_/byas te rigs gsum bsams nas su/_/spyan drang ba yi cho ga bya/_/de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rnams kyi/_/gsang sngags kun la dbul lo zhes/_/me tog spos chus bkang ba yi/_/mchod yon dag ni

[\[162b.4\]]rdzas su bshad/_/sngags kyi rgyud las ma gsungs kyang /_/blo dang ldan pas rdzas 'di rnams/_/rab tu drag po'i las dag la/_/cho ga bzhin du sbyar bar bya/_/sbyin sreg cho ga byas nas ni/_/slob ma dbang bskur 'os rig nas/_/cho ga bzhin du nan tan du/_/

[\[163a.1\]]shin tu bkra shis tshigs bcad bsgrags/_/de bzhin bkra shis rgya cher gdon/_/'byor par 'gyur ba'i sil snyan dang /_/glu dbyangs dag dang rnga sgra bsgrags/_/mdor na de la sogs pa yi/_/cho ga rgyas pa byas nas su/_/yid kyis

[\[163a.4\]]zhi ba'i phyir/_/rgyas pa'i cho ga shar du bltas/_/drag shul spyod pa de bzhin du/_/lho phyogs kha bltas brtson de bya/_/de ltar dbang bskur byas nas ni/_/de la sar pa'i gos rnams bskon/_/me tog dri la sogs pas mchod/_/mchod phyir thogs

[\[163b.1\]]sgrub pa po yang rgyud la sbyor/_/de skad bsgo nas de 'og tu/_/de nas slob ma de yi phyir/_/sbyin sreg cho ga sngon bzhin bya/_/yam sreg shing gi me la ni/_/dkyil 'khor bdag po'i gsang sngags kyis/_/mar gyi sbyin sreg brgya dag bya/_/de bzhin zhi ba'i gsang

[\[164a.1\]]'dun dang /_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang ni/_/rig sngags gsang sngags tshogs rnams la/_/dad pas rab tu brten par bya/_/rtag par phyag rgya chen po la/_/khyad par du ni mos par bya/_/dam tshig can dang mdza' bo dang /_/bla ma la yang gus

[\[181b.1\]]gtsang ma'am/_/lo ma bkrus pa'i gzhi bting nas/_/cho ga'i bye brag shes pa yis/_/phyi nas lha bshos dbul bar bar bya/_/pad+ma'i lo ma'am pa la sha/_/'o ma can shing las skyes pa'am/_/yang na ras ni sar pa'ang rung /_/zhi ba'i gding bar bsngags pa yin/_/
[\[181b.2\]]chu skyes 'dab ma thams cad dang /_/ljon shing lo ma gtsang ma'am/_/khur skya sa la bting ba dang /_/chu shing lo ma rgyas pa la'o/_/arga b+ha la ta ka dang /_/ljon shing kha bo'i lo ma'am/_/mkhas pas gang yang rung ba dag_/drag po'i don du gding bar bya/_/lo 'dab 
[\[181b.3\]]mo yi ming can rnams/_/rig sngags rnams kyis gding bar bya/_/mngag gzhug rnams la rtswa dag dgram/_/'dab ma sngon po sa la dgram/_/slob pa pos kyang cho ga 'dis/_/rab dang 'bring dang tha ma la/_/sa gzhi bskus shing bstan nas su/_/ci rigs su ni bya bar bshad/_/

[\[181b.5\]]tha mar zho dang 'o ma ste/_/'di dag lha bshos cho gar bshad/_/cho ga 'dis ni ma smos pa'i/_/lhag ma'ang khong du chud par bya/_/dkyil 'khor dag dang sgrub pa la/_/lha bshos nan tan bskyed de bya/_/des na mkhas pas lha bshos dag_/_mi ngan pa dang rgya cher bya/_/bsnyen 
[\[181b.6\]]pa'i dus na ci nus dang /_/ci skad bstan dang ci snyed pa'i/_/gtor ma'i las ni bya bar bstan/_/dus tshigs dag la bzang por bya/_/gang dag bsreg bya'i rdzas rnams dang /_/bdag gi kha zas gang yin las/_/thog mar de yi phud dbul te/_/cho ga shes pas bzlas brjod 
[\[181b.7\]]bya/_/ji skad bstan pa'i lha bshos dang /_/rdzas kyi rigs rnams ci 'byor pa/_/mkhas pa rnams kyis phul nas kyang /_/nyin gcig bzhin du bzlas brjod bya/_/lha bshos dbul ba gsang sngags kyi/_/zhal zas yin par bshad pas na/_/des ni rtag tu kha zas 
[\[182a\]]
[\[182a.1\]]sbyin/_/de phyir zlos pa dag gis dbul/_/rtsa ba rdo gu 'bras bu dang /_/lha bshos cung zad ci snyed pa/_/dus gsum du yang gsang sngags la/_/phul nas dngos grub thob par 'gyur/_/gal te zlos pas gsang sngags la/_/mchod pa'i bshos rnams 
[\[182a.2\]]ma phul na/_/de tshe rtsub cing mdog ngan la/_/bkres pa dag gis gdungs par 'gyur/_/lha bshos med na de yi sems/_/rtog pa dag kyang mang por 'gyur/_/lha rnams 'grub par mi 'gyur zhing /_/bgegs rnams kyis kyang zil gyis gnon/_/de bas nan tan 
[\[182a.3\]]cher bskyed de/_/gsang sngags 'khor dang bcas pa la/_/dus tshigs dag la ci 'byor ba'i/_/lha bshos legs par dbul bar bya/_/bsnyen pa'i dus na zlos pa pos/_/khang pa'i phyi rol khor yug tu/_/lha rnams kun la 'byung po yi/_/gtor ma gus par dbul 
[\[182a.4\]]bar bya/_/gang dag 'gal dang mi shis dang /_/gang dag ngan cing smad pa dang /_/gzhan dag mi gtsang gyur pa'i rdzas/_/lha bshos phyir ni thams cad spang /_/thams cad dang ni las kun la/_/lag pan rgya chen dbul bar bya/_/lha rnams kun la dbul ba'i bshos/_/
[\[182a.5\]]gsang sngags kyis ni mngon par bsngags/_/sman rnams bcud ni yi gar 'ong /_/sngags kyi zas kyi bcud 'di dag_/bdag gi dad pas 'bul lags kyis/_/bzhes nas bdag la dgyes par mdzod/_/A ha ra A ha ra/_sarba bid+yA d+ha ra pU dzi te swA hA/_sgrub pos dang 
[\[182a.6\]]por sngags 'di dang /_/rang gi sngags kyis yongs bzlas nas/_/bsangs pa'i lha bshos lha rnams la/_/cho ga bzhin du dbul bar bya/_/gzhan gyi lha bshos gzhan dag la/_/gang tshe ma 'byor nas dbul ba/_/de tshe rang rig gsang sngags kyis/_/de la yang ni mngon 
[\[182a.7\]]par bsngags/_/gtor ma'i cho ga rim par phye ba'o//_//zhi ba dang ni rgyas pa dang /_/de bzhin drag shul spyod pa ste/_/mdor na las ni rnam gsum du/_/gsang sngags kun la bsgrags pa yin/_/las ni rnam pa gsum char gyi/_/dngos grub gang gis myur 
[\[182b\]]
[\[182b.1\]]ba dang /_/nges par 'grub par 'gyur ba yi/_/cho ga de dag 'dir bshad do/_/byams pa'i dran pa nyer bzhag nas/_/dkon mchog gsum la gcig tu gzhol/_/zhi bar gyur pas zhi ba yi/_/bzlas pa'am yang na sbyin sreg bya/_/zla ba yar gyi tshes gcig nas/_/

[\[182b.3\]]ku sha'i khres kyi stan 'dug nas/_/byang phyogs kha bltas gtsang zhi bas/_/zhi ba'i cho ga bshad par bya/_/ba yi lci ba ma lhung bas/_/dus gsum dag tu der bskus la/_/me tog dkar po sil ma dag_/bkram pa byas na rab tu shis/_/nas dang 'o thug zho dag dang /_/'bras 
[\[182b.4\]]yos dag gam til dag gam/_/dur ba'am ku sha sngon po'am/_/pri yang ku yi me tog gam/_/sA lu'i chan nam ge sar ram/_/yang na me tog dkar bo'am/_/sha ma'i yam sreg shing dag gam/_/yang na dri zhim thang chu'ang rung /_/mchod sbyin dag gi ljon shing ngam/_/'o mar 
[\[182b.5\]]bcas shing lo ma can/_/yam shing rtse mo las skyes rlon/_/sbrang rtsi'am yang na mar yang rung /_/rtog pa las gsungs cho ga ni/_/de dang de la sogs pa spyad/_/zhi ba'i las la blo can gyis/_/ljon shing 'o ma can gyi me/_/rgyun bzhag mi la blangs nas su/_/me ni cho ga bzhin 
[\[182b.6\]]byas te/_/zhi ba'i las la bsreg byin na/_/dngos grub rab tu ster bar 'gyur/_/'o ma can gyi yam shing gi/_/me la yam shing mtho gang tsam/_/'o ma sbrang rtsi mar btags te/_/zhi ba'i las la sbyin sreg bya/_/dgon pa'i ba lang lci ba dang /_/de bzhin sha ma'i bud shing

[\[183a.1\]]de yi zhabs su 'khor lo bzhag_/de yang 'phang du sor gcig pa'o/_/pad+ma'i skyil krung du 'dug ste/_/blo yis bsgom pa byas nas su/_/mchod pa la sogs legs byas te/_/de nas zhi ba'i las bya'o/_/dang por ston pa thub chen dang /_/shes rab
