[\[195b.1\]]ldan gyur na/_/dngos grub chen po myur du stsol/_/dus mtshams dag la rig sngags rnams/_/spyan drang mchod pa byas nas ni/_/mchod yon mngon par bsngags pa yis/_/dbang bskur ba yang bya bar bshad/_/nyin re khrus byed tshe na yang /_/dbang bskur phyir ni gus 
[\[195b.2\]]pa ru/_/blo dang ldan pas snyim pa'i chu/_/bdun nam yang na gsum gyis bya/_/mar dang 'o ma la sogs pas/_/dbang bskur phyir ni legs bkrus nas/_/rig sngags gzir ba rgyas gyur cing /_/'dis ni lhag par tshim par 'gyur/_/lha dbang bskur ba'i cho ga rim 
[\[195b.3\]]par phye ba'o//_//dus mtshams dag la smyung byas nas/_/nub gcig gam ni nub gsum du/_/gtsang zhing gos dkar gsar bgos te/_/zlos pa sta gon gnas par bya/_/dus mtshams min yang dgos yod na/_/yar gyi ngo yi tshes bzang la/_/zhi ba'i 
[\[195b.4\]]mchog gi gsang sngags kyis/_/sta gon gnas par rab tu bya/_/skyu ru ra sogs khrus rtsi dang /_/dri zhim spos chus khrus byas te/_/nye reg byas nas srod la ni/_/sangs rgyas spyan drang mchod pa bya/_/de nas lhag par mngon bsngags pa'i/_/mchod yon cho ga bzhin 
[\[195b.5\]]du dbul/_/de nas tsan+dan dkar po dang /_/sna ma'i me tog kha 'bus dang /_/ma la ta yi phreng ba la/_/bdug pas bdugs la mchod pa bya/_/gtor ma mang zhing bzang ba dang /_/zho dang bcas pa dbul bar bya/_/de nas mar gyi sbyin sreg ni/_/tshul bzhin brgya rtsa 
[\[195b.6\]]brgyad byas te/_/gsang sngags las dang rjes mthun par/_/sa rdza ra sa'i sreg blugs dbul/_/bu mos bkal ba'i skud pa la/_/mdud pa bdun bor lan bdun bsngags/_/dpung pa g.yon pa la bcings la/_/ku sha'i lo ma bting ba la/_/de nyid kyis ni glo phab ste/_/
[\[195b.7\]]bka' lung gsol ba btab nas ni/_/rang gi lha yi tshul 'dra bar/_/sems kyis legs par bsam byas te/_/yid la gsang sngags 'don bzhin du/_/ku sha sar pa khres kyi sngas/_/me tog mang pos bklubs pa la/_/ci ltar bde bar nyal bar bya/_/gal te gnyid log rmi 
[\[196a\]]
[\[196a.1\]]lam na/_/bstan par gtogs pa'i lha mthong ngam/_/so sor rig pa'i gzugs dag gam/_/yang na rig sngags bdag po'ang rung /_/dkon mchog gsum las gcig tsam mam/_/de dag la ni mchod la sogs/_/rgyal sras rdzu 'phrul chen 
[\[196a.2\]]po'am/_/'khor ni rnam pa bzhi rnams sam/_/bdag nyid cho ga spyod pa'am/_/yang na gos kyis spud pa dag_/mthong na dngos grub nyer 'gyur bar/_/sgrub pa pos ni shes par bya/_/ri dang glang po 'bab chu dang /_/rgya mtsho dang ni 'bras bu shing /_/ngang mo la 
[\[196a.3\]]sogs bya rnams dang /_/seng ge la sogs [{]ri dgas [,]ri dwags [}]sogs/_/khyu mchog bkra shis rta la sogs/_/bu mo bzang mo brgyan pa dang /_/bum pa la sogs bkra shis pa/_/rnam pa sna tshogs g.yas na'o/_/nor dang gos rnams rnyed pa dang /_/de la sogs pa rnam dag pa'i/_/
[\[196a.4\]]rmi lam bzang po mthong na ni/_/blo can 'grub par shes par bya/_/zho dang 'o ma 'bras yos ma ra/_/me tog 'bras bu rtsa ba dang /_/yang na grub pa'i rdzas kyang rung /_/rmi lam dag na rnyed pa'am/_/de 'dra'i rnam pa mthong gyur na/_/rig sngags 'grub par gsungs pas na/_/
[\[196a.5\]]de nas blo dang ldan pa yis/_/bsnyen pa'am sgrub pa'i las rnams brtsam/_/gal te sngags kyi nor bu'am/_/sgrub pa'i rdzas rnams thob na ni/_/de nas bsnyen pa'am sgrub pa yi/_/las rnams myur du brtsam par bya/_/gos dang khrus dang rgyan dag gis/_/bdag nyid 
[\[196a.6\]]brgyan pa mthong na ni/_/de tshe bsnyen pa'am sgrub pa yi/_/las rnams rab tu brtsam par bya/_/rang gi rig sngags tshul bzhin du/_/mchod pa byas nas rigs yum gyis/_/sna ma'i me tog brgya dag dang /_/ras zung dag gis mchod par bya/_/tsan+dan gyi ni bdug spos kyis/_
[\[196a.7\]]lan brgyad nyin du bdugs nas ni/_/de nas lha nyid rmi lam du/_/ci rigs par ni bka' lan stsol/_/u shi ra yi gzugs brnyan ni/_/grog mkhar sa yi snod du bzhag_/mchod cing yongs su tshim byas nas/_/lan brgyad dag tu mngon par bsngags/_/de ni 'o ma'i 
[\[196b\]]
[\[196b.1\]]nang du 'am/_/yang na sbrang rtsi'i nang du gzhug_/dus gsum dag tu legs mchod nas/_/srod la yang ni gsol ba gdab/_/rnam pa 'di dag nyid kyis kyang /_/yongs su dgyes pa skyes gyur nas/_/de ltar bya 'am mi bya ba/_/lha nyid bka' lan gsol bar mdzad/_/

[\[196b.3\]]du bka' stsol to/_/de ltar rig pa sta gon gnas/_/nges shing myur du 'grub par 'gyur/_/sta gon gnas pa'i cho ga 'di/_/rgyas par rab tu bsgrags pa yin/_/sta gon gnas pa'i cho ga rab tu gsang ba'i rim par phye ba'o//_//slob mas dkyil 'khor phyag 
[\[196b.4\]]byas nas/_/khyad par du ni yon phul te/_/bla ma'i kha nas mngon sum du/_/rig sngags yongs su gzung bar bya/_/snyim pa me tog gis bkang nas/_/gus shing rim gro bskyed byas te/_/bla mas thog mar lan gsum bzlas/_/rang gis lan gsum bzlas te gdon/_/
[\[196b.5\]]de nas yi ge mang po'i sngags/_/gi wang dag gis shog shog la/_/ji skad bstan bzhin mngon bris te/_/de nas ci bder kha ton bslab/_/bla ma yongs su mgu ba las/_/dus mtshams dag gam tshes gzhan la/_/rig sngags brtags nas byin pa dag_/cho ga bzhin du 
[\[196b.6\]]gus par mnod/_/slob mas legs par mnod pa de/_/ring por mi thogs 'grub par 'gyur/_/ma bsnyen par yang de la de/_/rtag tu 'go zhing nye bar gnas/_/yang na gser la sogs pa yi/_/bum pa gsar zhing gtsang la bzang /_/skyon kun rnam par spangs pa la/_/
[\[196b.7\]]bkra shis ngo mtshar dag kyang byas/_/de la spos chu 'ba' zhig med/_/khyad par du ni bsham byas nas/_/gtsang mar byas te nub gcig gam/_/nub gsum du ni smyung byas te/_/srod la rab tu brtsam byas nas/_/cho ga 'di dag spyad par bya/_/gsang sngags rig sngags 
[\[197a\]]
[\[197a.1\]]gdams pa dag_/gro ga la sogs shog shog la/_/gi wang dag gis mnyam bris te/_/shog shog rnams ni lhan cig gzhug_/rig sngags rgyal pos legs par ni/_/dri dang me tog bdug mchog dang /_/de bzhin lha bshos mar me dang /_/sbyin

[\[197a.6\]]dang ni slob ma yis/_/rig sngags sbyin zhing yongs bzung ba'i/_/cho ga 'di ltar byas na ni/_/lha nyid rab tu 'grub par 'gyur/_/mkhas pas rig sngags 'grub pa kun/_/grub pa nyid du shes par bya/_/rnam pa de ltar rdzas dag dang /_/tshul bzhin thob pas bsnyen

[\[197b\]]
[\[197b.1\]]dang zho/_/'bru dang nor bu bu mo dang /_/mal cha rnams dang lham dag dang /_/rgyan gyi rnam pa thams cad dang /_/sgrub pa'i yo byad rnams dang ni/_/glang po ba lang rta la sogs/_/bkur sti rnam pa du ma dang /_/bdag gi bdog pa mtha' dag dbul/_/gus par phyag byas

[\[197b.4\]]gal te 'dir yang la la zhig_/yi ge lhag gam chad pa yi/_/dogs pa skyes na mkhas pa yis/_/gsang sngags bkang ba'i cho ga bya/_/shog shog dag la gi wang gis/_/gsang sngags yi ge tshang bar bri/_/cho ga bzhin du mchod byas te/_/rig sngags rgyal po mngon par

[\[197b.6\]]bdag po dang /_/rig sngags yid dbang phyug ma dang /_/bde gshegs sras bcas phyag byas te/_/bkang ba'i phyir ni gsol btab nas/_/rig sngags dran bzhin ku sha yi/_/stan la shar phyogs kha bltas nyal/_/rig sngags rgyal pos de nyid/_/mtshan mo dag ni 
[\[197b.7\]]nges par yang /_/yi ge gsal ba de dag dang /_/smyu gu yang ni de nyid dang /_/gi wang dag kyang de nyid kyis/_/shog shog kyang ni de nyid la/_/gsang sngags chad pa rab tu skong /_/lhag pa dag kyang mnyam par mdzad/_/gsang sngags ma nyams mnyam pa dag_/'ba' 
[\[198a\]]
[\[198a.1\]]zhig 'dri bar mi mdzad la/_/gsang sngags rig sngags ma tshang ba/_/nges par 'di yis skong bar mdzad/_/yang na yig 'bru ma tshang ba/_/rmi lam dag tu ston par mdzad/_/gsang sngags zlos pa po dag gis/_/bsrung ba'i cho ga byas te bya/_/rig sngags

[\[198a.3\]]dang /_/mar dang thang chu'i sbyin sreg gis/_/gsang sngags gzi byin che bar 'gyur/_/ba yi rnam lnga jos nas su/_/ri yi rtse mor ci rigs par/_/me tog 'bum dag dbul byas nas/_/des ni lha nyid gzi byin skye/_/nyin gsum du ni dus gsum du/_/dri zhim dri dang

[\[198a.5\]]dang /_/mchod pa dag dang lha bshos kyang /_/'dod pa pos ni khyad par du/_/lha rnams thams cad gzi chen 'gyur/_/lha gzi byin bskyed pa'i cho ga rim par phye ba'o//_//gang zhig gsang sngags zlos pa dag_/dngos grub chen po myur thob pa'i/_/sbyin sreg 
[\[198a.6\]]cho ga ma lus pa/_/de dag ci bzhin spyad par bya/_/lha yi gnas kyi phyi rol du/_/de yi mdun du mi ring bar/_/ci ltar rigs pas yongs brtags la/_/cho ga 'di dag kun du spyad/_/dbus su me yi thab brko ba/_/gru bzhi lham pa kha khyer can/_/khru gang zabs su khru byed 
[\[198a.7\]]pa/_/yang na thab khung zlum por bya/_/de nas yam shing la sogs pas/_/yo byad dgos pa thams cad dag_/g.yas phyogs su ni gzhag par bya/_/g.yon du chu yi snod bzhag go/_/de nas las kun byed pa yi/_/sngags kyis de dag bsang gtor te/_/'dug nas 
[\[198b\]]
[\[198b.1\]]mkhas pas gsang sngags rnams/_/yid la bsams te spyan yang drang /_/mchod yon yongs su bzlas pa yang /_/de dag rnams la phul nas su/_/me tog gcig gis rig sngags de/_/de nyid du ni bzhugs su gsol/_/de nas me ni bsang ba'i phyir/_/khro bo'i

[\[198b.3\]]zas bzhes nas kyang /_/'di nyid du ni bzhugs su gsol/_/o~M ag+na ye ha bya ka bya pA ha nA ya swA hA/_de ltar dang por me gnyer nas/_/sreg blugs gsum yang bsreg par bya/_/o~M ag+na ye ha bya ka bya/_ba ha na yA dI bya di pA ya swA hA/_de nas mkhas pas g.yas phyogs

[\[198b.5\]]rau dri pa tri ta/_ma hA kro d+ha bi dza ya ni kr-in+ta hU~M phaT ban+d+ha ban+d+ha swA hA/_de nas yam sreg shing dag bsreg_/de nas yam shing me la mar/_/de nas til dang 'bras chan te/_/cho ga de dag mdor bsdus pa'o/_/ba la sha dang n+ya gro d+ha/_/p+lak+Sha seng ldeng arga dang /_/be'u kang ka dang a mra dang /_/kar+m+ma 
[\[198b.6\]]ri dang sha mi dang /_/a pa marga las byung dang /_/u dum a shwat+thar bcas pa/_/yam shing bcu gnyis dag tu bstan/_/sar pa dag las mdzub gang tsam/_/las rnams kun la bsreg bya ste/_/las rnams kun la thor to gnyis/_/brtags nas rtse mos bsreg par bya/_/bzang la 
[\[198b.7\]]drang zhing gsar pa la/_/spos chus bsang gtor byas pa la/_/zhi ba'i bsreg bya cung zad gang /_/rgyas pa'ang gang dag yin pa dang /_/bdag zas cung zad gang yin pa/_/de dag las rnams kun la bsreg_/nyin re'am yam sreg shing dag la/_/bdag gi zas kyang rtag tu bsreg_/
[\[199a\]]
[\[199a.1\]]sngags dang ji ltar rjes mthun par/_/sbyin sreg byas nas kha zas bza'/_/bzlas brjod cho ga ji ltar gsungs/_/sbyin sreg la yang de ltar bsgrags/_/lag pas pus mo'i nang rol nas/_/sbyin sreg dag ni brtsam par bya/_/rig sngags thams cad gzi bskyed

[\[199a.6\]]rnams bya bar bshad/_/lag mthil chu la bzlas pas ni/_/lan gsum du yang 'thor 'thung bya/_/sbyin sreg byas pa'i tha mar ni/_/rang gi rig sngags nyid kyis kyang /_/bsang gtor lan gsum bya bar bshad/_/de 'og me la kun bsregs nas/_/spyan drang rig sngags 
[\[199a.7\]]de nyid kyis/_/bzhud cig bzhud cig ces byas te/_/de yi 'og tu slar btang ngo /_/gsang sngags yi ge'i rjes mthun par/_/mjug tu bzlas brjod brtsam par bya/_/de ltar sbyin sreg thams cad kyi/_/cho ga mdor bsdus bshad pa yin/_/sbyin sreg gi cho ga rim 
[\[199b\]]
[\[199b.1\]]par phye ba'o//_//de nas gzhan yang gang dag gis/_/bsdus nas rig sngags thams cad kyi/_/gsang sngags cho ga rtsom 'gyur ba'i/_/cho ga yan lag bsdu ba bshad/_/dgos pa'i yo byad thams cad ni/_/thog ma nyid du kun bsdus te/_/de nas bsnyen pa'am sgrub

[\[199b.3\]]bum pa dang ni zangs kyi snod/_/'bru dang rin chen sna lnga dang /_/sman rnams dang ni sbrang rtsi dang /_/de bzhin bu mos bkal ba yi/_/tshon sna lnga yi srad bu dang /_/mar me'i don du kong bu dang /_/shing bal mar me'i snying po dang /_/kham phor dang ni tshon rtsi'i rtsi'i rdzas/_/de bzhin

[\[199b.5\]]yos pri yang ku/_/tsan+dan dkar dang shing gi lham/_/muny+dza ku sha sha ta pus/_/me tog snod ni shis pa dang /_/mchod pa'i yo byad mchog dang ni/_/de bzhin bgrang phreng la sogs dang /_/de dag la sogs blo can gyis/_/nor dang sgrub pa'i yan lag rnams/_/thams cad

[\[199b.7\]]bshad par bya/_/yid bzhin nor bu bum pa bzang /_/nor gyi char 'bab gser chen dang /_/'khor lo ldong ros ral gri ste/_/'di dag dngos grub bdun yin no/_/phal cher spyi yin khyad par 'phags/_/che la mchog gi mchog yin te/_/de yi bsod nams phung chen dang /_/
[\[200a\]]
[\[200a.1\]]rgyal srid dag kyang thob par 'gyur/_/gzhan yang dngos grub dam pa ni/_/gtsug tor pad+ma rdo rje gsum/_/rigs dang rigs kyi bye brag las/_/phal cher yongs su bsgrags pa yin/_/gsang sngags gang yang rung ba yis/_/gang yang rung ba'i dngos grub kyang /_/
[\[200a.2\]]mngon par shes pa lhag rtog pa/_/gtso bo yin par yongs su bsgrags/_/gser dang dngul la sogs pa las/_/yu ba khru gang tsam byas la/_/de steng rin chen chen po ni/_/gcig pu bzhag pa'am nor bu ni/_/pad+ma ra ga dag pa'am/_/yang na shel las byung ba'ang rung /_/
[\[200a.3\]]khri'u'i steng du legs bzhag nas/_/sgrub pa pos ni mtshan mo bsgrub/_/gsang sngags sta gon cho ga dang /_/bdag nyid dbang bskur gang bshad pa/_/de yi rang bzhin cho ga des/_/bum pa bzang po bsgrub par gsungs/_/gser dag dang ni dngul dag dang /_/rin chen sna 
[\[200a.4\]]tshogs la sogs pa/_/dpag tshad lnga yi khor yug tu/_/nor ni char bzhin 'bab par gsungs/_/mi zad pa yi gter chen ni/_/gser la sogs pas gang ba ste/_/sbyin dang longs spyod la sogs pa/_/spyad cing phyung yang mi zad pa'o/_/ur mo'i lcags kyi 'khor lo ni/_/
[\[200a.5\]]mdzub gang tsam la rtsibs drug pa/_/shin tu gzugs legs rno bdar ba/_/myur du 'grub cing chen por 'gyur/_/nyi ma 'char ka'i gzugs 'dra zhing /_/gser ni btso ma'i mdog lta bu/_/ka ra bi ra'i mdog 'dra zhing /_/ldong ros dag ni mchog tu bshad/_/ral gri mthe'u 
[\[200a.6\]]chung mtho do ba/_/'phan med zheng du sor bzhi tshad/_/bdar ba tsa sha'i 'dab ma 'dra/_/'grub phyir ba so'i dngo can no/_/phyag rgya bri ba'i cho ga bzhin/_/gtsug tor phyag rgya gser las byas/_/yid bzhin nor bu'i yu ba byas/_/che la bzhag ste bsgrub par bya/_/pad+ma tsan+dan las

[\[200b.1\]]ba bla yon tan 'phags pa dag_/gser gyi gyim phag 'dra ba yi/_/sul gyis gang zhig ljid che ba/_/kha dog bzang po 'grub phyir mchog_/ser skya dag las byung ba yi/_/gi wang kha dog ser po'o/_/btsag ni yug snam gser mdangs can/_/me tog bam+du'i mdog 'dra 
[\[200b.2\]]ba'o/_/grog mkhar brtsegs pa 'dra ba la/_/btsag na ut+pal sngon po'i mdog_/shin tu 'jam po 'di 'dra ba/_/chu rgyun las byung any+dza na'o/_/ras phran gtsang ma 'jam po ni/_/kho lag che la gur gum btsos/_/dgon pa'i phyugs kyi lci ba yi/_/thal ba ga bur gyis 
[\[200b.3\]]bsgos pa'o/_/mchod phyir thogs kyi srad bu dkar/_/phra zhing sum bsgril legs bkal ba'am/_/yang na gser gyi skud pa ni/_/legs bsnyod sum bsgril yon tan can/_/sna ma'i me tog phreng ba ni/_/bu mos bkal skud las brgyus pa'o/_/shri pa Na yis shing gi

[\[200b.5\]]tu shis/_/'di ni cho ga las gsungs pa'i/_/bsgrub bya'i rdzas rigs gang yin pa/_/de dag mtshan nyid 'jig rten las/_/khyad par du ni nye bar brtag_/de bzhin dngos grub mang po yis/_/bsgrub bya'i rdzas ni sna tshogs pa/_/de bas de dag bdag blo dang /_/gtsug 
[\[200b.6\]]lag blo yis yongs su brtag_/nad med mdangs bzang lus ma nyams/_/gzugs bzang rma med dar la bab/_/bdag nyid shi bar gyur pa'i ro/_/ro langs dngos grub phyir ni mchog_/yang na las kyi bye brag las/_/rigs ngan dag kyang rab tu shis/_/ro langs ba sgrub

[\[201a.1\]]sngags nye bar gyur nas ni/_/gang tshe bka' lung gsal shes pa/_/de tshe bsgrub pa'i rdzas gzung ba/_/mkhas pa dag gis legs par bya/_/khrus byas gtsang zhing smyung byas te/_/bkra shis ngo mtshar dag byas nas/_/blo dang ldan pas bdag nyid kyis/_/

[\[201a.6\]]any+dza na ni 'ba' zhig go/_/ral gri 'khor lo la sogs rdzas/_/ba yi lci ba chu mang bas/_/shing dang sems can la sogs rdzas/_/thams cad ba yi gcin dang chus/_/[{]ri dgas [,]ri dwags [}]nag po'i pags la sogs/_/ba yi gcin dang bska bas bkru/_/de ltar rdzas rnams

[\[201b.1\]]pa'i gsang sngags sam/_/rigs dang rigs kyi snying po yi/_/gsang sngags rdzas dang mthun pa yis/_/thams cad sbyang bar bya bar grags/_/thams cad rigs kyi rig sngags kyis/_/bsang gtor byas na dag par bshad/_/dang po ba yi rnam lngas bya/_/de yi rjes la til

[\[201b.3\]]pa las/_/dngos grub phyir ni srang lnga'o/_/'bring po la ni srang gsum ste/_/tha ma dag la srang gcig go/_/gi wang dag ni srang gcig tshad/_/ba bla dag ni srang gnyis so/_/any+dza na ni zho drug ste/_/ba mar la ni srang bdun no/_/thal ba la ni srang lnga ste/_/gur gum ldong

[\[202a.1\]]las kyi cho ga yis/_/gsang sngags yongs su tshim byas te/_/dbang bskur cho ga gsungs pa'ang bya/_/de nas bsgrub pa brtsam par bya/_/dang por dkyil 'khor bris nas su/_/cho ga bzhin du legs mchod de/_/der ni bdag nyid tshul bzhin du/_/

[\[214a\]]
[\[214a.1\]]tu bsgrub par bya/_/rig sngags kyi ni lha yi rnams/_/dam tshig gis ni dkyil 'khor du/_/lhag par byin gyis rlob pa dag_/khyad par du ni 'byung bar 'gyur/_/rtag tu gus pas mnyes bya ba'i/_/cho ga 'dis ni dgongs 'gyur zhing /_/sgrub pa po 
[\[214a.2\]]dag 'dod pa yi/_/dngos grub thams cad stsol bar mdzad/_/'dir ni rigs kyi snying po dang /_/rigs kyi yum dang rgyal po dang /_/spyi yi bsrung ba'i gsang sngags kyang /_/dngos grub myur du stsol bar mdzad/_/dkyil 'khor gsum po 'di dag ni/_/gsang chen yin 
[\[214a.3\]]par yongs su bsgrags/_/rdo rje rigs kyi pho nya rdzas sgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rim par phye ba'o//_//de nas gzhan yang dkyil 'khor 'di/_/gsang chen snying por gyur pa ste/_/tshul bzhin rdo rjes mtshan pa yi/_/dkyil 'khor legs par bri bar bya/_/
[\[214a.4\]]dbus su rigs kyi rgya bris nas/_/de la rig sngags gzhag par bya/_/yang na bum pa gang ba ni/_/bkra shis sngon bzhin bshad pa bzhag_/de steng kham phor la sogs pa/_/kha sbyor nang du rdzas kyang bzhag_/shar du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/_/byang du spyan 
[\[214a.5\]]ras gzigs dbang phyug_/lhor ni bcom ldan rdo rje 'dzin/_/nub tu drag po nor bdag go/_/rig pa'i rgyal po'i tshul du ni/_/thams cad phyag rgya'i steng du dgod/_/rigs kyi rig sngags g.yas phyogs su/_/g.yon du las rnams kun byed pa/_/nub phyogs 
[\[214a.6\]]kyi ni ngos gnyis su/_/dkar sham ma dang dpal mo bzhag_/lhung bzed dang ni chos gos kyang /_/shar gyi grwa ni gnyis su bri/_/byang phyogs phyag na pad+ma yi/_/dbyug pa dang ni guN+Di bri/_/lho phyogs rdo rje 'dzin pa yi/_/rdo rje dang ni tho ba bri/_/nub phyogs kyi ni 
[\[214a.7\]]grwa gnyis su/_/rtse gsum nor gyi bum pa bri/_/sgo kar gzhan gyis mi thub ma/_/shar gyi phyogs su 'phrog ma bzhag_/lho yi phyogs su ri mkhar ma/_/byang du ral pa gcig ma bri/_/phyi rol lha rnams dgod pa ni/_/mdor na ci ltar 'dod pa bzhin/_/gsang 
[\[214b\]]
[\[214b.1\]]sngags mchod pa'i cho ga kun/_/snga ma bzhin du yongs su bsgrags/_/dkyil 'khor rab tu gsang ba 'di/_/sgrub pa'i tshe na bgegs med bshad/_/rdzas rnams kun dang las rnams ni/_/gsang sngags bdag gis ci dgar 'grub/_/bcug nas 'byung ba 
[\[214b.2\]]nyid kyis kyang /_/bgegs bya bar ni mi nus so/_/dri dang me tog bsung zhim dang /_/bdug spos mar me gsal ba dang /_/bshos kyang rnam pa sna tshogs kyis/_/de nas mchod pa legs par brtsam/_/bzlas brjod cho ga las gsungs dang /_/dkyil 'khor 
[\[214b.3\]]dag tu ci bstan pa/_/de bzhin khang pa'am dkyil 'khor du/_/mchod pa yi ni cho ga bya/_/rig sngags rgyal la lha bshos ni/_/snying por gyur pa sna tshogs dang /_/mchod pa sna tshogs gang yin pa/_/cho ga bzhin du bya bar gsungs/_/mar gyi mar me gsal 
[\[214b.4\]]ba dang /_/snying po dag kyang gsal bar dbul/_/'go bar bya ba'i ched du ni/_/rang rig sngags la mchod yon dbul/_/de nas rig sngags rgyal po yis/_/yungs kar dag la bsngags nas su/_/nad rims dag ni thams cad du/_/gsang ba'i bsrung ba rab tu 
[\[214b.5\]]bya/_/las kun byed pa'i rig sngags sam/_/yang na bsrung ba gzhan yang rung /_/yungs kar yongs su bzlas pa dag_/rdzas kyi drung du gzhag par bya/_/de yis kun du gtor ba yis/_/bgegs rnams las ni bsrung bar 'gyur/_/g.yon du rang gi phyag rgya 
[\[214b.6\]]bzhag pa'am/_/ral gri mngon par bsngags pa'ang rung /_/phyogs skyong phyogs su bzhag byas te/_/de'i mod smyung zhing bsrung ba byas/_/sems stobs che zhing gtsang sbra can/_/gos kyang de yi kha dog ldan/_/lus dang stobs dang lang tsho dang /_/gzugs dang ldan pa'i 
[\[214b.7\]]skyes bu zhig_/dpal la bzlas pa'i ral gri 'dzin/_/mgul nas phreng ba'i do shal 'phyang /_/yungs kar dag ni thu bar blugs/_/bgegs rnams blta la mkhas pa ste/_/phreng ba dang ni yungs kar dag_/bgegs la rab tu 'phen par nus/_/bgegs rnams kun nas 
[\[215a\]]
[\[215a.1\]]'byung ba'am/_/yang na 'jigs pa chen po la/_/'jigs pa med par ral gris bsdigs/_/gal te nye bar 'ongs nas 'debs/_/yungs kar dag dang phreng ba spos/_/bgegs rnams nye bar zhi bar 'gyur/_/yang na rang gi gnas dag na/_/legs 
[\[215a.2\]]par gnas pa'i ral gris bya/_/bskor ba'i gnas rnams bor na ni/_/skabs dang glags ni rnyed 'gyur zhing /_/de la bgegs kyang 'jug par 'gyur/_/de bas nan tan bskyed de bsrung /_/de dag sgrub pa'i cho ga las/_/bsrung ba'i las ni mdor bsdus pa'o/_/rgyud las 
[\[215a.3\]]gsungs pa'i yon tan can/_/phyogs skyong rnams ni ma rnyed na/_/lcags mda'a'am yang na mda' can dag_/bzlas nas phyogs su gzugs par bya/_/gsang sngags bzlas shing dka' thub can/_/rgyud 'dzin shes par ldan pa zhig_/gsang sngags sgrub pa'i grogs 
[\[215a.4\]]mchog ste/_/bzlas brjod byed cing sgo kar bzhag_/des ni bgegs ni bzlog pa dang /_/las rnams kun la 'jug par bya/_/rgyud rgyud dag las rang gi rgya/_/bsrung ba cis kyang mi tshugs gang /_/de dag bzlas shing mchod byas nas/_/bdag nyid kyis ni bcang 
[\[215a.5\]]bar bya/_/bgegs chen drag po rnams la ni/_/de dag gis ni bzlas bya'am/_/yang na 'dod pa'i gsang sngags kyis/_/bsngags pa'i yungs kar dag gis bya/_/lha yi dkyil 'khor phyi rol du/_/gtor ma'i cho ga ci rigs par/_/rab tu dang zhing bzang ba'am/_/
[\[215a.6\]]yang na 'byung po kun la bya/_/bskrad pa dang ni 'og bcing dang /_/steng yang bcing zhing khor yug tu/_/mtshams bcad phyogs kyang bcing bya zhing /_/rdo rje dra ba ra ba bya/_/rgyud dang slob dpon lung dag gis/_/rdzas dang bdag dang lha yang bsrung /_/gsang sngags dag gis 
[\[215a.7\]]phyi nang du/_/bgegs rnams thams cad bzlog par bya/_/cho ga de dag thams cad ni/_/phyi dro'i dus su bya bar bshad/_/nyi ma nub par gyur nas ni/_/rdzas rnams bsgrub pa brtsam par bya/_/blo dang ldan pa phyir byung nas/_/nye reg yang dang yang byas te/_/bdud rtsi 
[\[215b\]]
[\[215b.1\]]thab sbyor bzlas byas pa'i/_/spos chu khyor gang btung bar bya/_/dkyil 'khor bdag po'i snying po yis/_/bzlas pa'i mar ni cung zad btung /_/ngal dang snyom pa la sogs pa'i/_/gnod pa thams cad zhi bar 'gyur/_/stang zil sbrang rtsi pi pi ling /_/sangs 
[\[215b.2\]]rgyas spyan gyis bzlas pa'am/_/snga mas bskus na myur bar ni/_/bgegs las byung ba'i gnyid sel lo/_/bsdams shing shar du kha bstan 'dug_/lha rnams la yang phyag 'tshal nas/_/kun la yid kyis gsol btab ste/_/de nas sgrub la 'jug par 
[\[215b.3\]]bya/_/mtshan ma bzang po rnam pa gsum/_/bzlas brjod byed pas bzung nas ni/_/rab tu dga' ba'i sems kyis ni/_/de nas sgrub la 'jug par bya/_/mtshan ma dag ni ci 'dra las/_/dngos grub dag kyang de 'drar gsungs/_/de nas zlos pa'i mtshan 
[\[215b.4\]]ma yis/_/dngos grub bstan pa 'dod par bya/_/legs par grub byed ces bya ba/_/rig pa'i rgyal po'i blo bsams nas/_/bum pa sgo kar bzhag pa la/_/bskor ba dag kyang gus par bya/_/lha yi gnas su zhugs nas ni/_/de yi 'og tu phyag byas nas/_/
[\[215b.5\]]'go bar bya phyir thams cad la/_/mchod yon gyi ni bya ba bya/_/rig sngags rgyal po'am rgyal mo'am/_/yang na spyi yi snying po'am/_/rang rang sngags kyis ci rigs par/_/spyan drang ba yi cho ga bya/_/dkyil 'khor dag tu bya ba bzhin/_/rang gi phyag rgya legs 
[\[215b.6\]]par bstan/_/de ltar byas na rig sngags dang /_/gsang sngags mthu chen byin gyis rlob/_/rdzas ni kha cig rnam brtags pa/_/lag pa'i snyim pa'i nang du gzhug_/kha cig mchod yon snod du gzhug_/kha cig bum pa'i steng du'o/_/grog mkhar sa yi kham phor ram/_/
[\[215b.7\]]yang na lo ma bting bar bzhag_/bsgrub bya stegs bu la bzhag pa/_/gi wang bskus pa'i snod bcug ste/_/bzlas pa'i gnas su bzhag nas su/_/yungs kar dag gis mngon bsrung ste/_/blo can cho ga shes pa yis/_/me tog ta ma li yis mchod/_/brtan 
[\[216a\]]
[\[216a.1\]]par bya dang bsrung ba dang /_/byin bskyed pa ni gang bshad pa/_/ci ltar rigs par rdzas la'o/_/ma stongs par ni bya ba'i rigs/_/lha dang rdzas kyi bar dag tu/_/ci yang gzhag par mi bya'o/_/rdzas kyi g.yas g.yon gnyis su ni/_/bsrung 
[\[216a.2\]]ba'i rgya dang yungs kar bzhag_/bdug spos mchod yon gtor ma dang /_/zho dang mar me la sogs dang /_/bsgrub bya'i rdzas ni bzhag nas kyang /_/dkyil 'khor blta ba gzhag par bya/_/rdzas la mig gam lag pa yis/_/blta'am yang na brim par bya/_/
[\[216a.3\]]g.yo ba'i yid ni mnyam bzhag ste/_/blo dang ldan pas shub bur bzlas/_/'dir yang byin bskyed cho ga dag_/sngon bzhin skabs skabs dag tu bya/_/de yi mtshan mo thog thag ni/_/de bzhin rgyun mi 'chad par bzlas/_/mchod yon la sogs cho ga kun/_/dus 
[\[216a.4\]]gsum du yang bya bar bshad/_/'thor 'thung la sogs dgos pa la/_/de tshe rjes su bsgrub pa bzhag_/sgrub pa pos ni bsgrub pa na/_/rtag tu nye bar gnas par bya/_/sgrub pa po bzhin cho ga yi/_/lhag ma sgrub grogs mchog gis bya/_/bgegs chen rnams 
[\[216a.5\]]ni zlog pa la/_/rjes su bsgrub pa dag gis bya/_/des ma nus na bdag nyid kyis/_/yungs kar la sogs bzlas pas bya/_/shar phyogs nas ni char chen 'bab/_/'jigs su rung ba'i 'brug sgra sgrags/_/me yi phyogs su glo bur du/_/mtshams kyi 
[\[216a.6\]]snang ba nam langs bzhin/_/gshin rje'i phyogs nas 'ong ba ni/_/'chi bdag gzugs can 'jigs 'jigs blta/_/ral gri thogs shing sgra chen 'byin/_/sna chad lo ma mi thod du/_/mi yi khrag ni 'thung bar byed/_/mgo skra gyen du brdzes shing 'bar/_/gcin 
[\[216a.7\]]rgyang char bzhin 'bab pa yi/_/bsrung ba'i las rnams 'jig par byed/_/bden bral phyogs nas sems can mang /_/'jigs pa'i gzugs can tha dad pa'o/_/chu lha'i phyogs nas lha yi bad ga_/sprin dang bcas par 'brug sgra sgrags/_/rlung gi phyogs nas 
[\[216b\]]
[\[216b.1\]]tshub chen 'byung /_/gnod sbyin pho mo byang phyogs nas/_/dbang ldan phyogs nas tshogs kyi gzugs/_/steng nas mthu chen lha rnams 'byung /_/'og na sa 'gas g.yo bar byed/_/rdzas kyi dngos grub chen po la/_/de la sogs pa bgegs kyi rnams/_/nam 
[\[216b.2\]]gyi phyed na 'byung bar 'gyur/_/dngos grub chen po rnams la ni/_/bgegs kyang chen po nyid du 'gyur/_/phal la rjes su mthun pa yi/_/bgegs ni rnam pa sna tshogs 'byung /_/dus gsum dag gi dngos grub ni/_/tha ma 'bring dang rab tu bshad/_/dus 
[\[216b.3\]]bzhin byung na rab tu shis/_/de la zlos pa mi shis so/_/dro dang dud 'thul 'bar ba dag_/'grub pa'i mtshan mar bstan pa yin/_/'bar ba las ni sum char bshad/_/du ba la ni rim bzhin gnyis/_/drod las dngos grub gcig pu ste/_/de ni tha ma 
[\[216b.4\]]yin par bshad/_/kha cig gsang sngags mthu dag las/_/myur du 'bab par gyur pa'am/_/gal te bsgrub tshe thog mar ni/_/dngos grub kha cig 'od byung nas/_/de tshe rang rig rig sngags kyis/_/dngos grub mnan pa brtsam par bya/_/mis ni rig 
[\[216b.5\]]sngags rgyal ba yi/_/snying pos ba yi gi wang ngam/_/lag pas brim na dngos grub ni/_/mnan par 'gyur zhing brtan par 'gyur/_/mar ram yang na me tog gam/_/rdzas kyi rigs la bzlas kyang rung /_/de ltar man nam rdzas rnams ni/_/spyad na 
[\[216b.6\]]yon tan thob par 'gyur/_/dang por grub par gyur na ni/_/thog mar gnas par byas nas su/_/de nas mtshan mo'i lhag ma la/_/blo can bzlas brjod ci 'dod bya/_/dngos grub 'bring po dag la yang /_/cho ga de bzhin bya bar bshad/_/nam phyed dag 
[\[216b.7\]]na grub pa ni/_/spyad pa'ang de yi dus su bshad/_/dang po pa ni srod la ste/_/'bring po dag ni nam phyed na/_/dngos grub rab dag spyad pa ni/_/skya rengs 'char ka'i dus su'o/_/dang po pa ni nang par te/_/lhag ma gnyis la nges pa med/_/'bring po mtshan 
[\[217a\]]
[\[217a.1\]]mo spyad bya ba/_/nang par spyad par mi bya'o/_/dngos grub tha mar gyur pa dag_/nang par spyad par dgag pa med/_/dus las 'das pa'i nges pa'am/_/rim pa gzhan yang mi shes so/_/gang zhig nang par mi spyad la/_/gal te gnas pa'ang 
[\[217a.2\]]ma byas na/_/de ni dman ma bzhin bor ba/_/spyad zin pa zhes bya bar 'gyur/_/bsgrub pas bskul ba'i rdzas dag la/_/gsang sngags gzi brjid kun zhugs pa/_/dus las 'das pa'i nyes pa yis/_/phal cher yongs su spong bar 'gyur/_/mnan pa dag 
[\[217a.3\]]ni phyi nas yang /_/grub kyi bar du rung bar 'gyur/_/mnan te bzhag pa'i rdzas dag ni/_/ci ltar 'dod pa spyad par bya/_/gal te grub pa'i rdzas dag ni/_/nam yang spyad par ma byas na/_/de las gzhan pa'i dus mtshams la/_/bzlas pa yang byas spyad 
[\[217a.4\]]par bya/_/ma grub pa yi rdzas dag la/_/cho ga de nyid rab tu bsgrags/_/dus tshigs dus tshigs dag la yang /_/byin bskyed la sogs cho gas bsgrub/_/lo gsum gyis ni gang ma grub/_/de ni nams kyang mi 'grub bo/_/mchog tu gyur pa'i rdzas 
[\[217a.5\]]rnams la/_/cho ga 'di ni yongs su bsgrags/_/zla ba drug gis 'bring po rnams/_/dngos grub nye bar 'thob par 'gyur/_/chung ngu rnams la dus dag ni/_/gang yang nges pa med par bshad/_/ri mo yi ni lha rnams la'ang /_/cho ga 'di nyid bshad pa yin/_/yongs su 
[\[217a.6\]]gzung ba la sogs pa'i/_/cho ga'ang de las gzhan pa'ang bya/_/rdzas bsgrub pa'i cho ga rim par phye ba'o//_//sems can snang dang mi snang las/_/grub pa'i rdzas ma grub pa'i tshe/_/gal te phrogs par gyur nas ni/_/dkyil 'khor 'dir ni bri bar bya/_/tshes 
[\[217a.7\]]grangs mi dgos rgyu skar min/_/smyung bar bya ba'ang med par gsungs/_/mchog tu khro ba la gnas te/_/mod la dur khrod thal ba yis/_/gru gsum nub tu sgo gtod pa'i/_/dkyil 'khor 'di ni bri bar bya/_/de ltar bris nas phyi rol bskor/_/sgrub pa'i rig sngags 
[\[217b\]]
[\[217b.1\]]gzhag par bya/_/de nas shar du bcom ldan 'das/_/legs par grub byed ces bya ba/_/drag po gnod sbyin sde dpon ni/_/mthu chen rig sngags rgyal po dang /_/rdo rje khro bo rdo rje dbyug_/rdo rje khu tshur lcags kyu ma/_/rdo rje kI li 'jigs byed gzugs/_/ser 
[\[217b.2\]]skya dang ni thog thog gzugs/_/lug rgyud rnam rgyal nag po dang /_/de bzhin sgor ni dga' byed dgod/_/rdo rje sde dang dpung bzang dang /_/khro bo chen por grags pa rnams/_/de dag rim bzhin bkod nas su/_/mkhas pas mchod pa'i cho ga bzhin/_/me tog dmar la sogs 
[\[217b.3\]]pas mchod/_/gtor ma khrag dang bcas par gsungs/_/drag shul spyod pa'i cho ga 'di/_/sngon du bstan pa kun kyang bya/_/mkhas pas rang gi rig sngags lha/_/sgo kar mngon du phyogs bzhag la/_/dri zhim me tog dag gis kyang /_/cho ga bzhin du mchod par 
[\[217b.4\]]bya/_/phyi rol dkyil 'khor ci dga' bar/_/de dang rjes su mthun bya ste/_/lha ni drag po gang 'dod pa/_/mchod pa dag la sogs pa bya/_/snying po'i dkyil 'khor dbus su ni/_/drag shul spyod pa'i las kyi thab/_/gru gsum kha ran can byas te/_/sbyin sreg las 
[\[217b.5\]]ni brtsam par bya/_/me 'bar yam shing seng ldeng ngo /_/nim pa'am dur khrod nas skyes pa/_/rang gi khrag las btags pa dang /_/dur khrod thal ba sar pa'am/_/dug khrag yungs kar bsres pa dang /_/de nas ske tshe sreg blugs dbul/_/rdzas 'phrog pa yi phyir bsngos 
[\[217b.6\]]te/_/gzugs brnyan steng du gnas pa'am/_/yang na gzugs brnyan gtub gtub cing /_/mjug tu sbyin sreg dag kyang bya/_/khro bo'i cho ga shes pa yis/_/cho ga 'di ni bya bar gsungs/_/gsang sngags zlos pas skrag gyur nas/_/rdzas 'phrog pa ni rings par yang /_/
[\[217b.7\]]'phrogs pa'i rdzas ni khyer nas su/_/mngon du 'ongs te sbyin par byed/_/byed na de la mi 'jigs sbyin/_/zhi ba ci dgar rab tu bya/_/gal te zhi ba ma byas na/_/de tshe mod la 'chi bar 'gyur/_/yang na mi snang ba yi rnams/_/dkyil 'khor sgor ni rdzas kyang 'jog_/
[\[218a\]]
[\[218a.1\]]yang na zlos par 'dod pa'i rnams/_/rdzas dag lhag par ster bar 'gyur/_/rdzas 'phrog pa mod la dgug pa'i cho ga rim par phye ba'o//_//rdzas phrogs nas ni ring lon nas/_/dkyil 'khor 'dir ni bri bar bya/_/rigs gsum rnams 
[\[218a.2\]]kyi spyi yin te/_/dngos grub phyir ni las kun byed/_/thams cad du yang rig sngags rgyal/_/legs par grub byed ces bya ba/_/snying po'i dkyil 'khor dbus su ni/_/phyag rgya bris te dgod par bya/_/rdo rje khro bo khro chen dang /_/mA ma kI dang lcags kyu ma/_/
[\[218a.3\]]rdo rje khu tshur rdo rje'i tog_/rdo rje dbyug pa tho ba dang /_/'jigs byed lug rgyud kI li dang /_/rdo rje blo gros mi thub ma/_/gsang sngags khro bo pho nya mo/_/rmad byung pha rol gnon gang dang /_/'dod pa 'byor byed rta mgrin dang /_/phyag na zhal ras phal chen dang /_/
[\[218a.4\]]bcom ldan sna tshogs gzugs can dag_/snying po'i dkyil 'khor dag tu dgod/_/grags ldan ma dang dpal mo che/_/dkar mo dang ni gos dkar can/_/sgrol ma zla ba dpal mo gang /_/rmad byung pha rol gnon rnams dang /_/'khor los sgyur sogs gtsug tor dang /_/
[\[218a.5\]]mdzod spu dang ni bde gshegs spyan/_/mche ba mdung thung byams ma che/_/rmad byung pha rol gnon gang dang /_/gzhan gyis mi thub la sogs pa/_/rigs kyi rig sngags bstan pa dang /_/las kun byed pa'i gsang sngags dang /_/phyag rgya chen por grags pa dang /_/
[\[218a.6\]]phyi rol bsrung ba'i sgo ba dang /_/cho gar gtogs pa gang yin pa'i/_/so so'i rigs kyi mang ga gzhug pa/_/brtson 'grus chen po dgod par bya/_/phyi rol 'jig rten skyong ba dang /_/tshangs pa mes po chen po dang /_/dbang phyug chen po chung mar bcas/_/tshogs 
[\[218a.7\]]spyan tshogs dang lhan cig tu/_/ma mo rnams dang klu bdun dang /_/de bzhin lha min bdag po dang /_/bstan pa la ni gang dga' ba/_/rmad byung pha rol gnon kun dang /_/dkyil 'khor snga mar gsungs pa yi/_/lha ni gang dang gang yin dang /_/gsang sngags 
[\[218b\]]
[\[218b.1\]]cho gar gang bstan pa/_/de kun phyi rol mchod par gsungs/_/de nas de yi 'og tu ni/_/cho gas sngon bzhin me sbar te/_/rdzas 'phrog gzugs brnyan spra tshil las/_/byas te slob ma'i steng bzhag nas/_/sbyin sreg cho ga bya bar gsungs/_/der ni glor 
[\[218b.2\]]yang bzhag nas su/_/mtshon cha yis ni gtub gtub cing /_/mjug tu tshul bzhin bsreg par bya/_/sngon bzhin mchod pa'i cho ga dang /_/gtor ma yi ni las kyang bsgrags/_/phyag na rdo rje'i rigs de yi/_/cho ga kun gyi drag shul spyad/_/de bzhin rang gi rig sngags 
[\[218b.3\]]kyis/_/cho ga drag shul bya bar gsungs/_/nyi shu brgyad la ma thob na/_/rdzas phyir dgra la drag shul spyod/_/mar gyi ngo yi tshes lnga la/_/cho ga byas pa de mchog go/_/lcug lcag gis ni dgra gzhu zhing /_/de bzhin mes kyang gdung bar bya/_/sna tshogs tshig gis 
[\[218b.4\]]brgyan pa dang /_/mda' yi tsher ma rnon pos dbug_/ske tshe lan tshwa byugs nas su/_/ci dga' bar ni yan lag gtub/_/dgra bo la ni cher khros pa/_/ci ltar 'dod pas chad pas gcad/_/dar ras dmar pos dkris nas su/_/skud pa dmar pos bcing bar 
[\[218b.5\]]bya/_/me tog dmar pos mchod bya zhing /_/ji srid 'dug gi bar du ni/_/rdzas kyi phyir ni bskul bya zhing /_/nyin gcig bzhin du bzhu bar bya/_/gal te des ni de byin na/_/de tshe chad pas gcad pa bshol/_/rdzas ni bstan pa 'di dag gis/_/nam gyi phyed na sbyin 
[\[218b.6\]]sreg bya/_/ko bi da ri'i yam sreg shing /_/'bru mar bstegs pa me la bsreg_/rang gi khrag dang dug dang bcas/_/yungs kar lan tshwar bcas pa dang /_/ske tshe de la bstegs pa yi/_/sbyin sreg brgya ni rtsa brgyad bya/_/rdzas 'phrog pa yi ming dang ni/_/rang

[\[263a.1\]]shis gang byung ba/_/bkra shis des ni skye dgu rnams la zhi byed shog_/lo ma me tog 'od 'bar nyams dga' lum bI'i tshal/_/lha mang dag gis bsten par mgon po bltam pa na/_/srid pa'i mthar phyin pa yi bkra shis gang byung ba/_/bkra shis des ni
